# EstreGenesis Changelog

Each tier (Master / Lite / Compact) has its own version. Master is the authoritative evolution track; Lite and Compact are derived regularly from Master but may lag by a release.

This file is the **changelog SSoT** — each seed file keeps only a compact header metadata line with tier, language, current version, counterpart, and a pointer back to this `CHANGELOG.md`, not the target project's README. When you upgrade a project using Migration B, the agent uses the seed header version marker plus this changelog to compute the delta.

**Language**: **English** (below) · [한국어](#한국어)

---

<a id="english"></a>

## Changelog (English)

- **v2.5.117** (2026-06-16) — **Greatpractice v0.3.2 — §B.5/§B.6 normative-foundations backfill (P0b complete)** — the two abridged Appendix-B placeholders (the §B.7 P0b "modality 2-axis full research" condition) are expanded into full subsections grounded in adversarially cross-checked primary sources, and **two v0.1 over-claims are corrected**. **§B.5 (distributed cognition)** separates the Clark-Chalmers *parity principle* (motivating) from the operational coupling criteria, and elevates C&C's own *crucial-vs-arguable* ranking (constancy/accessibility/automatic-endorsement "crucial" vs past-endorsement "arguable") to the primary-source warrant for the mandatory-vs-advisory tier split; **correction** — the criteria are framed as *necessary quality criteria, not a sufficiency test*: the cognitive-bloat objection (Rupert 2004; Adams & Aizawa, *The Bounds of Cognition*, 2008; Allen-Hermanson 2013) shows reliability + accessibility + trust are "satisfied far too easily", so a codified store is *embedded* (a resource leaned on — the coupling-constitution fallacy bars treating reliance as constitution), not literally constitutive. **§B.6 (institutional isomorphism)** keeps Douglas's "social control of cognition" + DiMaggio & Powell's three mechanisms (coercive/mimetic/normative, "not always empirically distinct") as an *analytic* bridge to the enforcement tiers; **correction** — the v0.1 "isomorphism inhibits innovation + ≤20% mandatory cap" claim is downgraded to *empirically contingent*: Hambrick et al. 2004 (*Isomorphism in Reverse*) found ~2× more intra-industry heterogeneity than homogeneity (18 industries / 162 regressions), Heugens & Lander 2009 found social-structure influence "weak" and conformity net-not-harmful, and Beckert 2010 found the mechanisms directionally indeterminate (the iron cage "may not exist at all") — and the **≤20% numeric cap is retracted** as having no evidence base (no quantitative threshold exists in the literature; the discipline is qualitative — keep the mandatory tier minimal + condition-aware). **§B.7** marks the P0b condition ✓ complete; the full Appendix-B → normative-foundations *body* promotion and the §4.5 numeric-cap removal remain for the v0.2 cut (entry conditions a/b still pending). Surfaces: `Greatpractice.md` frontmatter + title + §B.5/§B.6/§B.7 · plugin.json · marketplace (entry + metadata 0.3.23→0.3.24) · docs (greatpractice.html hero + meta, index module-tag) v0.3.1→v0.3.2 · EG badge / data.js → v2.5.117. **No runtime/schema change** — spec-content backfill + corrections. verify-nway 15-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.116** (2026-06-15) — **Constellation v2.4.38 — Compendium wiki tab (the v0.2-d dashboard surface)** — the live-board dashboard gains a **Compendium wiki tab** (a desktop top-tab + the reserved mobile #4 slot — the §11 board surface for the Compendium module). It renders the content store via a static `/compendium.json` export (derived by `plugins/compendium/lint.cjs --reindex`, served as a static file — **no server endpoint, no restart**), with a **dual-register plain/expert gloss toggle** (쉽게↔전문, localStorage-persisted), `owner_spec`→owning-spec pointers, register tags (내부어/일반어), and a **cross-link click-to-define** jump that scroll-highlights the target entry. Render is `esc()`-only post-escape per §8.1 (no raw HTML). Deployed via `sync-dashboard` (reference→public, client-side only); **Playwright-verified on the live board: 0 console errors, 7 entries, dual-register toggle + pointers + cross-links all functional.** `lint.cjs` now also emits the machine-readable `compendium/index.json` (a derived artifact, like INDEX.md). Compendium module unchanged at v0.2.1 (the wiki tab is a Constellation board surface). Remaining v0.2 polish: the cross-link side panel + the full a11y component (§8.2) + full ~25-term seeding. verify-nway 15-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.115** (2026-06-15) — **Compendium docs page + site nav (v0.2-c)** — the public module page `docs/compendium.html` lands, with the same tri-audience (general/dev/expert) EN/KO chrome as the other module pages; static content only — the concept-anchored dual-register model, the pointer-not-paraphrase charter, the v0.2 content store + lints + 8-tool MCP runtime, eviction/self-eviction, and the adoption thresholds (no fabricated metrics or charts). The `index.html` Compendium card now links to the page (was the GitHub spec), its stale "v0.1.0 design draft" prose is corrected to the v0.2 runtime state, and `Compendium` is added to the nav of all six docs pages for consistency. Compendium joins the verify-nway docs-badge + docs-meta axes (page hero badge + meta version checked against the `Compendium.md` frontmatter). Module version unchanged (v0.2.1 — a docs/presentation cut). verify-nway 15-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.114** (2026-06-15) — **Compendium v0.2.1 — MCP runtime (§10 8-tool server)** — the v0.2-b runtime increment: `plugins/compendium/mcp/server.cjs`, the §10 tool surface over the `compendium/` content store as a 0-dep line-delimited JSON-RPC stdio server (EG house MCP pattern; serverInfo.version from package.json). Eight tools: `wiki_read` · `wiki_search` (matches `hidden_search_only` labels for messy-input recall) · `wiki_upsert` (validates §4.1 frontmatter + §9.2 pointer-resolution + no-competing-full-def + the §2.2 redaction gate, then writes + re-lints) · `term_define` (term→definition + register-targeted gloss — the click-to-define backend) · `term_frequency_scan` (`store`/`docs` scopes scan real files; `conversation` READ-only) · `term_promote` (runs the §7.1 count→queue gate — occ≥10 ∧ sources≥3 ∧ mono-sense → a Hyperbrief brief stub; internal-register rejected per §7.3) · `compendium_backlinks` (derived inbound) · `compendium_lint` (the §9 lints + pointer-resolution). 8-tool smoke PASS. `mcp/package.json` joins the Compendium plugin-version axis (plugin + marketplace + mcp, all 0.2.1) and compendium joins the verify-nway serverInfo axis → verify-nway is now **15-axis**. Deferred to v0.2-c/d: docs/compendium.html, dashboard wiki-tab + side-panel + click-to-define, full ~25-term seeding. verify-nway 15-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.113** (2026-06-15) — **Compendium v0.2.0 — runtime foundation (content store + lint/pointer-resolution runtime)** — the first runtime increment of the Compendium module (v0.1 was a design draft — spec only). Ships: (1) a `compendium/` **content store** — 7 seed entries (5 glossary + 2 concept) materialized from the spec's Appendix A/B exemplars, each `owner_spec` pointer reconciled to a real spec heading-slug (ack-tier → `Constellation.md#1313-…`; the spec's illustrative `#3-key-management` was wrong); (2) `plugins/compendium/lint.cjs` — the §9.1 four gardening lints (broken-link · orphan · duplicate-concept · stale) + the §9.2 pointer-resolution check (owner_spec heading-slug grep-resolution + no-competing-full-def + redaction), 0 npm deps, `--reindex` regenerating the computed-MOC `INDEX.md`; (3) the §9.2 check wired into `verify-nway-version.cjs` as a new axis (requires the inner lint module — single source of logic) → verify-nway is now **14-axis** (the spec's "13th axis" label was its v0.1 framing; the *form* is fixed, the ordinal drifted). Compendium v0.1.0→v0.2.0 across frontmatter / plugin.json / marketplace / docs card. Deferred to v0.2.x: MCP server runtime (§10), dashboard wiki-tab + side-panel + click-to-define (§11), full ~25-term seeding. verify-nway 14-axis PASS · compendium-lint 0 hard.
- **v2.5.112** (2026-06-15) — **README module-count self-contradiction fix** — the public README's body advertised "three optional referenced modules (Constellation + Superscalar + Hyperbrief)" in two spots (EN + KO) while its own top section and the docs site already said **six** — a self-contradiction on the project's most-read public surface, made more wrong by the Greatpractice / Ultrasafe / Compendium ships. Both lines corrected to "six … (Constellation + Superscalar + Hyperbrief + Greatpractice + Ultrasafe + Compendium)". README-only; no version surface or module change. verify-nway 13-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.111** (2026-06-15) — **Constellation v2.4.37 — §13.x spec-body coherence pass (5 contradictions + 5 dangling refs + version-namespace convention)** — the deferred `hold-constellation-contradictions` track (0300-audit U4 list) resolved; **spec-body coherence only — the §2 wire contract is byte-unchanged**. (1) **Ack-tier reconciliation** — `AckProcessed` appeared at three different tiers across the spec (commitment in the §13.13 v2.5.2 mapping, application/"completed" in §13.19.7, "strongest grade/completed" in the §13.13 delivery-grades list). A single canonical reconciliation note now fixes `AckProcessed` = **commitment-tier** (the agent has surfaced/engaged, *not* completed — completion is the application tier `Report`/`DONE`/`BLOCKED`), maps the two parallel naming schemes (delivery grades `delivered`/`read`/`processed` ↔ escalation tiers `transport`/`commitment`/`application`) onto one model, separates the orthogonal pending-clear axis (§13.13.2), and documents the trivial-ask case §13.19.7/§13.19.9 rely on; the §13.13 grade list and the §13.19.7 table now cross-reference the SSoT note. (2) **Watcher-filter sync (§13.16.6 ↔ §13.16.9)** — §13.16.6's inline meaningful-inbound filter had drifted from its declared §13.16.9 SSoT: `AgentHello` moved to the noise blocklist (handshake group per the 4-group reclassification), and the Hyperbrief decision-delegation family + the Ultrasafe pre-release-pentest family + `PRRequestRejected` added to the meaningful allowlist; an explicit "§13.16.9 wins on divergence" precedence note now prevents re-drift. (3) **5 dangling cross-refs fixed** — §6.5→§13.22.6 (`sourceContentRef.kind`), §13.8→§2 (reply-window), §11.1→§13.16.9 (Hyperbrief `decided` ack-tier), and two bare `Ultrasafe.md` refs qualified to §16/§17. (4) **Version-namespace convention codified** — `v2.4.x` = Constellation module version · `v2.5.x` = EG release · `v0.x` = protocol, disambiguated by inline-tag prefix and paired 1:1 in CHANGELOG. No wire/field/state-machine change. verify-nway 13-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.110** (2026-06-15) — **Compendium v0.1.0 — the 6th module (design draft)** — EstreGenesis's vocabulary-substrate module lands: a concept-anchored dual-register glossary (one concept → one register-neutral definition + register-tagged terms/glosses; the expert↔plain mapping is implicit in the shared `concept_id`, never a brittle term-A↔term-B link) + a cross-module wiki + a cross-link/click-to-define system. It owns nothing normative — every entry is a one-directional pointer into the owning module spec (SSoT); the sole exception is general-register vocabulary no module owns. The purest expression of north-star axis-2 (vocabulary survival > code survival), and the relocation home for deprecated vocabulary (axis-3 eviction first-class) — it even models its own eviction. Right-sized per an adversarial design review: v0.1 ships the model + content-boundary charter + ~25-term EG seed exemplars + 4 gardening lints + a pointer-resolution check, with promotion reduced to a single count→queue-Hyperbrief-brief gate and the hysteresis/debounce automation, a11y component, multi-tab split, MCP runtime, and dashboard surfaces deferred to v0.2+ as named prunable units. Registration: `plugins/compendium/` manifest + marketplace entry (5→6 plugins) + verify-nway Compendium plugin-version axis + README/docs module count 5→6 (`docs/index.html` "Six graduated modules"). Seed-registry inclusion is deferred until production (design-draft). Spec: `Compendium.md`.
- **v2.5.109** (2026-06-15) — **Greatpractice + Ultrasafe specs translated to English** — the `Greatpractice.md` and `Ultrasafe.md` module specs, whose prose had drifted to Korean while the foundational specs (Constellation / Hyperbrief / Superscalar) stayed English, are now fully English to match — a consistency pass for the public standard-proposing surface. **No semantic change**: a 1:1 line-for-line prose conversion (Greatpractice 1056/1056, Ultrasafe 2507/2507 insert/delete; every heading, code block, YAML key, version number, §-reference, table, and citation preserved verbatim — structural verify of heading/fence/table counts is identical to source). The only Korean retained is the functional voice-linter regex match-targets in Greatpractice §6.3/§12.3 (translating them would break the lapse-detection patterns). Module versions unchanged (Greatpractice v0.3.1, Ultrasafe v0.2.2); this is an EG-release doc cut, not a module bump.
- **v2.5.108** (2026-06-14) — **docs meta-description version drift + verify-nway 12th axis** — the per-module `<meta name="description">` version stamps in the docs pages had silently drifted, uncovered by any verify axis: constellation v2.3.23→v2.4.36, hyperbrief v0.5.6→v0.7.0, greatpractice v0.1.0→v0.3.1, ultrasafe v0.2.1→v0.2.2; index.html still advertised "three graduated modules" (→five). The README KO heading read "3 선택 모듈" (→5), and the install-block plugin versions were stale (Constellation v0.2.3→v0.3.16, Hyperbrief v0.5.6→v0.7.0, Greatpractice v0.1.0→v0.3.1, Ultrasafe v0.2.2 added) with "all four"/"넷"→"all five"/"다섯". A new **docs-meta axis (12th)** checks each page's meta version against the module's frontmatter canonical version plus the index module count, so this surface can no longer drift uncaught. Module versions themselves unchanged (stamp-only fix). verify-nway 12-axis PASS, 0 drift.
- **v2.5.107** (2026-06-13) — **Constellation v2.4.36 — mobile realtime group swipe (#3a B)** — the behavioral half (B) of the confirmed mobile nav restructure (A = the v2.4.31 bottom tab bar). At ≤560px the realtime pane's content area becomes a horizontal **scroll-snap pager** — one page per channel group (업스트림/메인/보드워커/로컬/협업, each the group's time-ordered merged view). **Swiping** switches group-by-group, and the tab bar **selection + horizontal scroll follow** (bidirectional sync); a dot strip under the pager indicates the current group. **Tapping** a tab (group header or channel) auto-scrolls the pager to that group's page. Desktop (>560px) is untouched — single `#ws-stream`, no pager. Implementation: `wsRenderActiveStream` was refactored into a container-parameterized `wsRenderStreamInto`, and group computation was factored to `wsComputeGroups` so the tab bar and the pager share the exact same group set/order; a 560px `matchMedia` toggles modes; swipe-settle is detected via a debounced `scroll` listener with a programmatic-scroll guard (tab-tap scroll ≠ user swipe — no feedback loop); live rows re-render only the active group page (cross-group rows just bump the unseen badge). No duplicate-render hazard — each channel belongs to exactly one group page (pages are groups, not channels). Playwright 390×844: swipe→group switch + tab-bar follow + dot indicator, tab→pager scroll, 0 console errors; board smoke 13/13 (no regression). Mobile-only, needs on-device testing. Reference dashboard (index.html/app.js/style.css); no protocol surface. verify-nway 11-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.106** (2026-06-13) — **Constellation v2.4.35 — mobile realtime pane fullscreen gap fix** — a follow-up to the v2.4.31 mobile bottom-tab restructure, caught via Playwright on a real 390px viewport: the realtime pane left a ~16px strip on the right and a band at the bottom where the page background showed through. Root cause (found by inspecting computed geometry, not guessing — `width`/`100vw` overrides kept resolving to 374px): the desktop `.ws-pop` carries `max-width: 96vw` + `max-height: 92vh` caps, which clipped the mobile fullscreen pane to 374×776 inside a 390×844 viewport. Fix: the ≤560px rule now sets `max-width: none` + `max-height: none` (alongside `width:100vw`/`height:100dvh`), so the pane fills the viewport edge-to-edge; the bottom tab bar overlays via z-index and the pane body keeps its bottom padding so the input stays above it. Verified exact 390×844 fill (popRect right=390, bottom=844). Reference dashboard (style.css); no protocol surface. verify-nway 11-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.105** (2026-06-13) — **Constellation v2.4.34 — dashboard UI/UX polish (Playwright-verified)** — three visual fixes found by a live Playwright loop (desktop 1366 + mobile 390, 0 console errors), split out of the v2.5.104 XSS cut that had swept them in via `git add -A`. (1) **Realtime header title no longer char-wraps** — on a narrow mobile header the bold "실시간" stacked vertically (실/시/간); `.ws-pop-head > b { white-space: nowrap }` keeps it on one line and the agent-name meta ellipsis-truncates instead. (2) **Mobile cards no longer cramp the title** — the planned/done card `.row` (number + title + chips + action + reorder) squeezed the title to one-word-per-line; at ≤560px the row now wraps so the title takes a full line and the chips/buttons flow below. (3) **Group merged-view label fixed** — selecting the board-worker (or collab) group showed "로컬 그룹" in the connection line (a `grpName` fallback gap); both are now mapped. Reference dashboard (app.js/style.css); no protocol surface. Adds reusable `scripts/pw-board-smoke.cjs` (catches load-time regressions like the v2.4.31 TDZ). verify-nway 11-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.104** (2026-06-13) — **Constellation v2.4.33 — dashboard XSS patch (audit U2: 2 real residuals)** — the 2026-06-10 full-audit Phase-2 (track 0300) U2 confirmed two residual XSS sinks the v2.5.72/75 sweep missed, both in the reference dashboard: **(1) `attNewTab` new-tab blob** — the mermaid path interpolated `${a.body}` *raw* into a `text/html` blob opened same-origin (`<pre class="mermaid">${a.body}</pre>`), and the html path opened `a.body` raw — a mermaid/html attachment body like `</pre><img src=x onerror=…>` executed in the board origin on the operator's "new tab" click; **(2) `decisions[].previewUrl`** rendered as `<iframe src=…>` with no `sandbox` and no scheme allowlist, so a `javascript:` previewUrl executed same-origin. Fixes: new-tab mermaid now `esc(a.body)` (mermaid reads the decoded textContent so rendering is unchanged), new-tab html now renders inside a `sandbox` iframe (matching the in-dialog policy); a new `wsSafeUrl()` scheme allowlist (http/https/blob/mailto/data:image + relative; everything else → `#`) guards the previewUrl iframe (+ `sandbox` added), the link-attachment iframe src, and the `window.open(a.src)` img/link/file path. `decisions[].previewHtml` raw-innerHTML is left as-is (operator/main-authored, safe-by-design but coupled to the S1/S3 board-write-auth boundary — flagged, not independently patchable here). `wsSafeUrl` unit-checked 11/11; board smoke 13/13 (no regression). U1 (S8/S9 WS-frame DoS, S10 MCP ajv/path) reconfirmed already-closed (v2.5.71 frame caps + v2.5.75 ledger-path confinement) — no patch. Reference dashboard (app.js); no protocol surface. verify-nway 11-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.103** (2026-06-13) — **Constellation v2.4.32 — hotfix: syncMobileTabbar TDZ (v2.4.31 regression)** — the v2.4.31 mobile-tabbar wired `syncMobileTabbar()` into `applyPanes()`, which runs once at top-level load **before** the `wsState` const is initialized; `syncMobileTabbar` reads `wsState.popOpen`, so that early call threw `ReferenceError: Cannot access 'wsState' before initialization` — an *uncaught* error that halted the whole `app.js` and left the dashboard blank. Fix: `syncMobileTabbar` now reads `wsState`/`ui` inside a try/catch and returns early if they are still in the temporal-dead-zone (the initial `applyPanes` no-ops the sync; `setupMobileTabbar` + later renders sync correctly once state exists). Lesson: the `applyPanes` guard checked the *function's existence* (hoisted, always true), not its *internal early-state access* — guarding existence ≠ guarding the body. Reference dashboard (app.js); no protocol surface. verify-nway 11-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.102** (2026-06-13) — **Constellation v2.4.31 — mobile bottom tab bar (realtime joins as a tab)** — the structural half (A) of the confirmed mobile nav restructure. At ≤560px a fixed bottom tab bar appears — `[대시보드][검토사안][위키][실시간]` — and becomes the top-level navigation: the top `.topbar` tabs and the floating 💬 FAB are hidden, and **the realtime view (formerly a floating popup) joins as a bottom tab** — selecting 실시간 opens the fullscreen realtime pane, selecting 대시보드/검토사안 closes it and shows that pane. The bar's active state syncs from `ui.panes` + `popOpen` (hooked in `applyPanes` + `toggleWsPop`). 위키 is a disabled placeholder for #4 Compendium. The realtime pane leaves room for the bar (bottom inset); `main` gains bottom padding; home buttons lift above the bar. **Desktop (>560px) is untouched** — top tabs + floating popup as before. Mobile-only, needs on-device testing. Remaining #3a: (B) group-level swipe inside the realtime tab. Reference dashboard (index.html/app.js/style.css); no protocol surface. verify-nway 11-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.101** (2026-06-13) — **Constellation v2.4.30 — group-member checkbox filter (merged view)** — when a channel tab GROUP is selected (the time-merged stream of its members), the source-filter bar now shows a per-member checkbox (☑/☐, default all checked) so you can pick which members' content appears in the merge — e.g. show only board-worker + Main↔Board while hiding the rest. Hidden members are tracked per group (`wsState.grpFilter`, default empty = all shown); toggling re-renders the merge. Desktop + mobile common (the first piece of the refined swipe/nav spec; the bottom-tab-bar + 실시간-as-tab + group-swipe restructure is mobile-only, queued next). Reference dashboard (app.js/style.css); no protocol surface. verify-nway 11-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.100** (2026-06-13) — **Constellation v2.4.29 — responsive mobile (realtime window fullscreen)** — the #3a mobile-layout pass. At ≤560px the floating realtime window goes **fullscreen** (`inset: 0 !important` to override the JS-restored inline position/size; resize handles hidden), the channel tab bar becomes horizontally scrollable (no wrap), and the header/body gain safe-area-inset padding (notch/home-bar). Extends the existing 720px/460px breakpoints. CSS-only (reference style.css); no JS/protocol surface. Remaining #3a: swipe-to-switch tabs (implementation approach pending — full scroll-snap content re-architecture vs lighter touch-handler). verify-nway 11-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.99** (2026-06-13) — **Constellation v2.4.28 — tier-1 dashboard notifications (§13.24.2)** — the #3a notification layer. A 🔔 settings dropdown in the realtime header carries a master toggle (which requests `Notification` permission) + per-item toggles (검토요청 / A2A 수신 / 작업 오류·중단), persisted to localStorage. On **live** (non-replay) events the dashboard fires `new Notification` (icon = the board's PWA icon, click focuses the window): a newly-appeared unresolved decision (tracked by a `renderDecisions` seen-set, first render suppressed so existing items don't alert), a meaningful A2A message (`a2acard` rows, hooked once in `wsPushRow` after the replay guard), and `RUN_ERROR`. Replay/History never alerts (the `wsState.replaying` guard). This is the "human-gate → OS" surface — a notification shortens the human-response latency that Superscalar's agent-time-vs-human-time thesis is built on. Tier-2 Web Push (background, PWA closed) remains staged for #3b. Dashboard-local (reference index.html/app.js/style.css); no protocol/server surface. verify-nway 11-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.98** (2026-06-13) — **Constellation v2.4.27 — installable PWA foundation + configurable board title (§13.24)** — two related dashboard surfaces. **(1) PWA (#3a foundation)**: the reference dashboard ships `manifest.webmanifest` + `sw.js` (app-shell network-first cache so updates land immediately; live data `/api`·`/ws`·`/join` bypassed; `notificationclick` focuses the window) + square 192/512 icons (any + maskable, generated from the deployment's symbol with an 8% safe-zone pad) + `index.html` wiring (manifest/icon/theme-color links + SW registration). The static server's MIME map gains `.webmanifest` (`application/manifest+json`) + `.png` (a board restart applies it). Tier-1 connected notifications + tier-2 Web Push are staged (#3a/#3b). **(2) Board title customization (formal)**: `backends.json` gains a board-level `boardTitle` field (default `Constellation`); the dashboard applies it to the topbar brand (`#board-name`) + document title at load, and `sync-dashboard` templates the *deployed* manifest `name`/`short_name` from it — so the title is deployment config, not a source fork point. EG self-board → `EstreGenesis`. Reference dashboard (index.html/app.js/manifest/sw/icons) + reference server MIME. verify-nway 11-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.97** (2026-06-13) — **Constellation v2.4.26 — tab-edit drop-position indicator** — a follow-up polish to v2.4.25's tab-edit reorder: dragging a group or tab now shows a vertical insertion bar at the exact spot where it will land on release, instead of just outlining the hovered target. The bar tracks the cursor's left/right half of the target to pick insert-before vs insert-after, and the reorder splice honors that side; every `dragover` clears all indicators first so there is no boundary flicker. Reference dashboard (app.js/style.css). Dashboard-local UX, no protocol surface. verify-nway 11-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.96** (2026-06-13) — **Constellation v2.4.25 — dashboard tab-edit reorder mode** — the realtime window gains a tab-edit toggle (top-right, `⇄`) that exposes a reset button (`↺`) and makes tab GROUPS (drag the group header) and TABS (drag the tab) reorderable by drag-and-drop. Group order + per-group tab order persist to localStorage (`constellation-ws-taborder`); reset clears back to default. Group vs tab drags are isolated by distinct drag MIME types so they never cross-fire; tab reorder is within-group only (cross-group drops are no-ops, preserving the role grouping); ordering uses a stable decorate-sort so unsaved items keep their natural order. In edit mode the per-tab close (✕) and tab-switch click are suspended (drag-only). Dashboard-local UX — zero protocol/server surface. Reference dashboard (app.js/style.css/index.html). verify-nway 11-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.95** (2026-06-13) — **Constellation v2.4.24 — backend registry + board-worker projection (§13.23, C1)** — the C1 absorption from the netwaif/multi-agent-starter benchmark, adjusted EG-native. - **v2.5.94** (2026-06-13) — **Superscalar v0.5.0 — topology pattern catalog (§1.5, divergence / reconvergence vocabulary)** — the C2 absorption from the netwaif/multi-agent-starter benchmark, adjusted EG-native (concept/vocabulary only, no code copy — north-star axis 2). A new §1.5 names the two SIMT-lineage primitive verbs — **divergence** (work splits into concurrent lanes; richer than plain fan-out, spanning homogeneous *and* heterogeneous splits) and **reconvergence** (the lanes merge back) — plus three reconvergence *modes* (**synthesis** = combine into a new whole / the existing synthesis barrier; **retire** = in-order commit / the existing §3 retire; **review** = one lane gates another). The starter's four patterns (Pipeline / Fan-out·Fan-in / Expert Pool / Producer-Reviewer) are then *recognized*, not added, as the divergence→reconvergence shapes the existing issue_width / lane-class / retire / Hyperbrief-interlock machinery already expresses, each pinned to its mechanism so an operator can request a shape by name. Speculation (§4) is reframed as *speculative divergence* that may be squashed before reconvergence; the Constellation board (§6) projects the divergence→reconvergence shape. starter attribution (MIT) per the EstreUX external-framework rule. Surfaces: Superscalar.md frontmatter + docs/superscalar.html (hero + meta) + docs/index.html module-tag, all v0.4.3 → v0.5.0. **No wire change**. verify-nway 10-axis PASS.

Post-compaction re-injection is already owned by the SessionStart(matcher:"compact") hook that re-reads the whole handoff file, so the PreCompact half only needs to write the snapshot: it now writes the file and exits with a schema-valid `{suppressOutput:true}` (confirmation routed to stderr). - **v2.5.87** (2026-06-12) — **Constellation v2.4.19 — /drillnow skill (top-blocker depth drill)** — plugin 0.3.16. The depth counterpart to `/roundnext`'s breadth: pick the single highest-priority blocked item and spend the turn *actually trying to clear it*. Contract: a drill ends in exactly one of two states — the blocker is gone and the work has started, or the blocker is **proven** unclearable right now and the queue is re-prioritized around that proof; "still blocked, unchanged" is not a valid exit. Procedure: ① target selection (top blocked item; user-decision gates are excluded — they belong to the decisions panel, not to drilling); ② blocker decomposition into this-side-doable / other-party / environment / time parts (recorded blockReasons are routinely coarser than reality); ③ escalating clearing attempts — re-verify (already gone?) → this-side prerequisite work → alternative/partial route → tool substitution → §13.20 nudge one tier up with the drill's findings attached, all under §13.18 gates; ④ exit A: unblock + start now; ⑤ exit B: state the immovable part + what/when will move it, demote the item, promote the doable work the drill surfaced, and rewrite `blockReason` to the decomposed verified form — the next drill starts from truth, not a stale coarse reason; ⑥ report the delta. A drill that merely re-describes the blocker has failed its contract. **No wire change**. verify-nway 10-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.86** (2026-06-12) — **Constellation v2.4.18 — dashboard UI setup-time localization MUST (§6)** — doc-only, plugin unchanged. The reference dashboard ships Korean-original: ~1,900 hardcoded UI string spans (buttons, labels, tooltips, status copy) across `app.js`/`index.html`, with no localization guidance anywhere in the spec — only locale-sensitive *behaviors* (client-local timestamps §13.11.3 rule 3, date-line day labels) were normative, and those are language-independent. New §6 rule: when an adopter sets up the board for a user whose prevailing language is not Korean, the setting-up agent MUST localize the UI strings as part of setup — the setup agent is an LLM that already knows the user's language from the surrounding conversation, so a faithful one-time pass needs no i18n infrastructure (display strings only; identifiers, wire vocabulary, CSS classes, event names, and §13.14-redaction-checked content are untouchable). Same discipline family as Hyperbrief §5.6.7 auto-localize, applied to the board surface — closing the asymmetry where one module had a normative language rule and the other none. Optional for mixed-language teams: extract to an i18n dictionary (the EG promo site under `docs/` carries a working EN/KO pattern to copy) — registered as a planned item, not required for the single-language common case. **No wire change**. verify-nway 10-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.85** (2026-06-12) — **Constellation v2.4.17 — stop-hook registry-path fallback chain (cwd-independent session routing; cursor-steal regression fix)** — runtime-only, plugin unchanged. The v2.4.7 register-all session routing resolved its registry at `<cwd>/.agent-sessions.json` — a trap: when an agent ends a turn while `cd`'d into a nested repo (e.g. an inner public repo inside the workspace), the hook misses the workspace-root registry, reports `registry=none`, and falls through to the legacy no-routing path — where the main session's hook advances *worker-owned* inbox cursors, the exact cursor-steal v2.4.7 was built to prevent (observed live 2026-06-12; no content was lost because the worker had already consumed the affected lines, but the protection had silently lapsed). Fix: `resolveRegistryPath()` searches a fallback chain — `AGENT_SESSIONS_PATH` env → cwd → `CLAUDE_PROJECT_DIR` → up to four parent directories of `INBOX_PATH` (the workspace root is embedded in the inbox path regardless of where the agent has wandered). All-absent preserves the legacy single-session behavior. Reproduced the failure condition (inner cwd, no env) → now `registry=active · session-route OWN`. **No wire change**. verify-nway 10-axis PASS.

- **v2.5.83** (2026-06-12) — **Constellation v2.4.15 + Hyperbrief v0.6.2 — /roundnext skill + decisions-panel fallback button (§5.6.7 board surface)** — plugin constellation 0.3.15 / hyperbrief 0.6.2. **(1) New plugin skill `roundnext`** — mechanizes the composition of §13.16.6 element 5 (planned-queue scan) + §13.20 (blocker tracking/nudge) + §13.18 (autonomous execution) into one invocable round, 5 steps: ① ripeness-check unblocked planned items and start what is ready; ② re-verify blockers *now* (recorded blockReasons go stale silently) — unblock, start, or re-sort; ③ for surviving blockers, derive what would clear them and which part is doable from here — register as planned or start if small (BlockerNudge cadence armed otherwise); ④ multi-dimensional new-work scan (release surfaces · doc/spec drift · verification gaps · security follow-ups · dogfood evidence · cross-module · undecomposed user intents) with an anti-inflation rule; ⑤ route human-gated items to the decisions panel as a Hyperbrief briefing, default tone L1.1.1 unless the project pins another level. A round never ends as a silent no-op — its delta (or why there is none) is the report. **(2) Hyperbrief §5.6.7 live-board surface (v0.6.2)** — the decisions panel becomes the third fallback surface alongside HTML/MD: every non-resolved decision card renders a tone-floor fallback button (label from the entry's `fallback.label`, populated from the IR's `audience_profile_fallback.button_label` per the auto-localize discipline; plain default otherwise); clicking POSTs `{kind:"fallback-rerender", id, question}` to the board feedback channel, and the brief-owning agent regenerates the entry's `detail` one floor lower — the MD trigger-phrase contract, board-mediated. - **v2.5.82** (2026-06-11) — **Constellation v2.4.14 — pre-compact handoff mechanization (§13.16.6 element 6 hook pair + before-compact skill)** — plugin 0.3.14. Compaction fires outside agent control and its summaries reliably drop *procedural* details — env-var call conventions, routing rules, policy one-liners, resume handles. Observed failure (2026-06-11): a required env-var prefix on one script call lived only in-context, was dropped by a compaction summary, and the post-compact agent reverted to the script's default path — misrouting five A2A messages to the wrong board until a human noticed downstream. **New reference runtime** `constellation/reference/runtime/pre-compact/`: (a) `pre-compact-snapshot.cjs` — `PreCompact` hook (matcher `*`): deterministically snapshots environment truth (git HEAD / dirty / latest tag, optional secondary repo + track-doc listing) into a two-zone handoff file and emits `additionalContext` directing the post-compact agent to read it; (b) `reload-handoff.cjs` — `SessionStart` hook (matcher `"compact"`): prints the handoff file to stdout for harness re-injection into the fresh context. The handoff file pairs a machine-replaced **auto-snapshot block** with a model-maintained **standing card** (the half no script can collect — what in-context details are load-bearing). **New plugin skill `before-compact`** populates the standing card: procedure conventions / in-flight cycle anchors / unrecorded decisions / active resource IDs + resume handles, with a keep-it-short discipline (the file re-enters context after every compaction — length is a recurring tax) and a promote-to-durable step. Spec note added under §13.16.6 element 6 (division of labor: hooks own environment + re-injection, the model owns judgment; this is what makes §13.21 operative at the procedural layer). **No wire change**. verify-nway 9-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.81** (2026-06-11) — **Superscalar v0.4.3 — §3.2 resume cache (journal-backed re-issue of interrupted fan-outs) + §11 Entry 07** — doc cut, plugin v0.1.2 unchanged. **New §3.2**: CPU mapping = checkpoint / precise-exception recovery. A wide fan-out interrupted mid-flight (token/session budget exhaustion, harness restart) after some lanes retired should not force full re-dispatch: a journal-backed resume cache replays each retired lane's `(prompt, opts) → result` from the journal and runs only un-retired lanes live. Harness-neutral discipline, three demands: (1) **determinism precondition** — referentially stable orchestration scripts (no wall-clock, no randomness, inlined static work-lists) or the cache key drifts; (2) **idempotent lane side-effects** — a real crash window exists between artifact-written and retirement-journaled, so artifact-writing lanes must tolerate re-execution (journal = retire SSoT, artifact presence = advisory); (3) **cost-benefit composition** — above the ~30-60k token dispatch horizon, resume capability is a prerequisite-grade harness feature; the manual fallback is per-item completion files + a skip-existing pre-check. Reference impl: Claude Code Workflow resume. **New §11 Entry 07** (n=1, incidental): a 53-lane read-only translation fan-out hit a session budget wall at 25 retired / 28 harness-failed; one re-issue recovered 25 lanes from journal (zero re-execution), idempotently overwrote 9 lanes caught in the artifact-vs-journal crash window, and ran the rest live — 53/53 + verification PASS, zero content loss. Validates both §3.2 preconditions in one incident. **No wire change**. verify-nway 9-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.80** (2026-06-11) — **Greatpractice v0.3.0 — retire axis (§7.7: active / probation / retired state machine)** — the GP-side implementation of EG's north-star value axis 3 (deprecation as a first-class operation): a standard that cannot shed cruft becomes precisely the burden its cleaner successor inherits, so retiring a practice must be as first-class as promoting one. **New §7.7**: a minimal 3-state `status:` frontmatter enum — `active` (default) / `probation` (validity in doubt — §7.3 validation failure, §5.6 miss-counter threshold, or suspected environment change; hooks keep enforcing but tag messages) / `retired` (enforcement stops; body preserved with mandatory `retire_reason` + optional `superseded_by`). Four transitions only (over-design forbidden): active→probation and probation→active are automatable; probation→retired and active→retired (direct, when superseded — with a §5.5 redirect stub) require user ratification, symmetric with promotion. Explicitly orthogonal to the existing `lifecycle` habit-formation axis (`lifecycle: probation` = "still young" vs `status: probation` = "under suspicion" — the combination `lifecycle: automatic` + `status: probation` is valid) and to §7.6 cold eviction (idle-driven vs validity-driven). **INDEX rule**: retired entries leave the tier sections; a one-line `Retired: N` counter preserves the ≤300-token cap. **Surfaces**: Greatpractice.md §7.7 + §7 cross-deps + `_schema.md` `status`/`retire_reason` fields + `INDEX.md` Retired stub. Hook-runtime status-scan exclusion lands with the runtime build (per §11 cut scope). **Module versions**: Greatpractice v0.2.1 → **v0.3.0** (plugin.json / marketplace / docs module-tag + hero badge synced). **No wire change**. verify-nway 9-axis PASS.

Previously `esc(a.body)` only prevented attribute breakout while the srcdoc interior rendered as a full HTML document same-origin → `<script>`/`onerror` executed + dashboard DOM/cookies reachable via `window.parent` (no sandbox). **(2) mermaid attachment `textContent` injection** — injects the raw diagram body via `.textContent` instead of `innerHTML`. mermaid.run reads the element's textContent as the diagram source so render behavior is identical, but the old innerHTML path let `<img onerror>`/`<script>` execute same-origin before mermaid parsing. **Playwright verification 5/5 PASS** (`assets/audit-2026-06-10/pw-dashboard-xss-smoke.mjs`, outer): mermaid SVG renders correctly (no textContent regression) + mermaid `<img onerror>` does not execute + html iframe carries the `sandbox` attribute + in-iframe script's `parent.__htmlXss` access blocked. **Files changed**: `constellation/reference/dashboard/app.js` (inner) + outer `collab-self/public/app.js` synced on both sides (node --check PASS) + Constellation.md (frontmatter v2.4.12 codicil) + plugin.json (0.3.12) + marketplace (0.3.18 + constellation 0.3.12) + README + docs/index.html (v2.5.72 + module-tag v2.4.12) + data.js (shipCount 88) + CHANGELOG. **Module versions**: Constellation v2.4.11 → **v2.4.12** (patch — dashboard render only, **no wire change · no server restart needed**, browser refresh only), plugin v0.3.11 → v0.3.12. - **v2.5.71** (2026-06-10) — **Constellation v2.4.11 security hardening patch (seed+module+plugin full-audit follow-up)** — per direct user instruction (2026-06-10: security/remediation/improvement-level items proceed as patch bumps; pruning-class and minor-bump-or-larger items go to separate review), of the reference-runtime security findings identified in the full audit (Workflow `wf_fe661e2b-c4c` — 10-area parallel survey completed + Phase 2/3 hit the session limit so main synthesized directly + core security code spot-check ✅verified), the 3 **patch-level (code fix / fact correction, no wire change)** items: **(1) secure-by-default bind** — reference `server.cjs` now binds `127.0.0.1` (loopback) by default (`WS_BIND` env override) + non-loopback startup warning. **Rationale (✅code-verified)**: the KEY-MGMT gate on board connections (`server.cjs:532` `if (isAgent && wsAgentRole!=='main')`) uses `isAgent &&`, so a board connection that never sent HELLO bypasses the gate entirely → unauthenticated KeyIssue/KeyList/KeyRevoke/SetMain (`:769-770` fall-through), while RegisterUpstream/CollabKey (`:527-528`) · SetMain (`:540`) have no gate at all. board=trusted-operator is intentional, but the previous `server.listen(PORT)` (`:796`, no host argument) = 0.0.0.0 bind meant LAN exposure → anyone could issue keys / list keys (KeyList returns collab/upstream in plaintext `:369-379`) / SetMain. Plus HELLO `msg.agentId` is unvalidated (`:705`) with a `'main-agent'` default (`:262`) → role spoofing. **The default loopback bind blocks this remote vector (critical + high×2) in one stroke** (gate/agentId-role redesign affects the wire → separate review). **(2) WS frame cap** — `ws-core.cjs` `decodeFrame` terminates immediately when the declared length > `WS_MAX_FRAME` (default 16 MiB), and the fragmented-reassembly total (`_fragLen`) gets the same cap — blocks memory-exhaustion DoS via huge declared lengths / unbounded continuation accumulation (the v2.4.5 2.5GB runaway class). **(3) credential gitignore + server-keys.eux correction** — `key.json` (keyStore) + legacy `ws-keys.json` + `local-keys/*.key` were not covered by `.gitignore` (`git check-ignore` exit 1 ✅) → plaintext key files could land in a tracked directory. Added the `.gitignore` block (now passes ✅) + corrected `server-keys.eux`'s single-file error of `KEY_JSON='ws-keys.json'` to an explicit 3-file listing. **Files changed**: `server.cjs`+`ws-core.cjs` (inner) + outer `collab-self/server.cjs`+`ws-core.cjs` synced (node --check PASS) + `.gitignore` + `server-keys.eux` + `Constellation.md` (§2 secure-by-default note + frontmatter v2.4.11 codicil) + README + docs/index.html (v2.5.71 + module-tag v2.4.11) + data.js (shipCount 87) + marketplace (0.3.16→0.3.17 + constellation 0.3.11) + plugin.json (0.3.11). **Module versions**: Constellation v2.4.10 → **v2.4.11** (patch — runtime security hardening, no wire change to default behavior: the board=loopback assumption matches the existing dogfood setup, WS_BIND/WS_MAX_FRAME are additive env), plugin v0.3.10 → v0.3.11. Other modules unchanged. Seed-tier v2.4.3 unchanged. **No protocol wire break**. cut closure: verify-nway PASS. - **v2.5.70** (2026-06-08) — **Constellation v2.4.10 A2A PR System §13.22 distill + deadlock server automation opt-in** — two normative reinforcements (direct user directive 2026-06-08: "apply the PR system, and add the server-side deadlock automation as an optional item that Constellation adopters can apply if needed"). **(1) §13.22 A2A PR System promoted to formal spec** — distills the previously dangling §13.22 reference at `Constellation.md` line 740 (reference existed with no section body) from the RRP design document (`constellation/reference/docs/2026-06-01-a2a-pr-system-rrp.md`, 972 lines) into a §13.19-grade formal normative section: **two-level abstraction** (Level 1 = A2A-only **virtual PR** — propose/review/merge negotiation over board A2A alone, without a git provider; Level 2 = **Github PR** provider-mediated — local-bridge creates/merges the actual PR) + **5 wire vocabulary** (`PRRequest` proposal / `PRDraftReady` draft ready / `PRReviewAck` review / `PRMergeRequest`·`PRMergeAck` merge negotiation / `PRStatusUpdate` status) + `sourceContentRef.kind` enum (inline / attachment-ref / mirror-branch / patch) + **fail-safe reject** of unrecognized kinds + **topology b** (agents have no direct git access — routed via local-bridge commands) + **approval discipline** (trusted-mirror auto-approve / standard opt-in **default** / emergency override) + **β′ mirror-branch-on-target** sourcing (mirror branch on the target repo, not the source repo) + **per-repo authority** (strict: only `role==main` passes the merge gate) + **5-state lifecycle** state machine (requested→draft→review→merge-pending→merged/rejected) + composition with §13.13 (at-least-once relay) / §13.19 (deadlock) / §13.20. EG **ships the protocol spec only** — the PR-bot reference impl is adopter-side (provider tokens/permissions live in the adopter environment). **(2) §13.19.10 Q3 deadlock server detector opt-in reference impl** — adds a board-adapter strict 2-cycle detector to `runtime/server.cjs`, `WS_DEADLOCK_DETECT` env-gated (**default OFF**): when enabled, approximates wait-edges via a reply-pairing map (`_a2aPending`) → on detecting a strict 2-cycle where both sides exceed the threshold (`WS_DEADLOCK_PROBE_MS`, default 120s), emits a `DeadlockProbe` CUSTOM to the board (duplicate suppression via `_deadlockSeen` Set + auto-clear when the cycle resolves, scan interval = min(probe, 30s) unref). Default OFF so **server↔application coupling is not forced** — **canonical detection remains the agent-side turn-start wait-edge DFS (§13.19.3)**, and quasi-deadlock remains agent-side SLA discipline (§13.19.4); the server detector is strictly a supplementary safety net (it approximates from observable reply-pairing only, so false negatives are possible — explicitly non-canonical). **Files modified**: Constellation.md (frontmatter v2.4.9 → v2.4.10 + codicil; new §13.22 section distilled after §13.21; opt-in reference impl paragraph after §13.19.10 Q3); plugins/constellation/.claude-plugin/plugin.json (v0.3.9 → v0.3.10 + desc); .claude-plugin/marketplace.json (metadata 0.3.15 → 0.3.16 + constellation v0.3.9 → v0.3.10 + desc); constellation/reference/runtime/server.cjs (WS_DEADLOCK_DETECT detector — both inner + outer collab-self/server.cjs, node --check PASS); README(badge + Current/현재 EN+KO); docs/index.html(hero badge v2.5.69 → v2.5.70 + module-tag v2.4.9 → v2.4.10); docs/shared/data.js(v2.5.70 + shipCount 85 → 86); CHANGELOG. **Module versions**: Constellation v2.4.9 → **v2.4.10** (patch — spec distill + server opt-in detector, **no default-behavior wire change**), plugin v0.3.9 → v0.3.10. - **v2.5.68** (2026-06-08) — **Constellation v2.4.8 dashboard EstreUF-parity 5-gap port** — ported 5 EstreUF-only behaviors identified via full comparison against the upstream original (EstreUF) dashboard (3-agent parallel, function/CSS/id inventory diff + inline behavior cross-check). EG was mostly equivalent or actually ahead (wsConfirm custom dialog · key-management kind dropdown/local-worker keys · anchor-based positioning · settings modal · context menu), and only the following 5 were EstreUF-only: **(1) hide decisions badge at zero** — `renderDecisions` toggles `_decBadge.hidden = (unresolved+adhoc === 0)`. Previously only `.textContent` was updated without toggling `.hidden`, so the `#decisions-badge[hidden]{display:none}` CSS was dead code → the tab showed a red "0" pill at all times even with zero decisions. **(2) preserve message send-time** — `wsMsgEpoch(m)`(m.timestamp epoch → m.at ISO Date.parse → null) + `wsRowTime(m)` helpers derive `_t`(HH:MM:SS)·`_ts`(epoch) at the top of onWsEvent → unified across all row pushes (status/user/TEXT_MESSAGE_START/TOOL_CALL/Attachment/a2acard/selection). Previously `_msgT` covered only the m.at number case + `row.ts=Date.now()` always + some `nowHM()`, so **after refresh/History replay all date-change lines collapsed to "today" + group-merge ordering followed receive order + per-card times within the same stream were inconsistent** → now uniformly pinned to the original send time. **(3) closed-session permanent-delete cross-board sync + persist** — added a `DeleteChannelHistory` handler to the server (`runtime/server.cjs`) (`wsCloseChannelHist`(remove history file) + `wsToBoards`(broadcast to other boards), mirroring the existing CloseChannel handler pattern) + inbound `DeleteChannelHistory`(synced channel removal) / `HistoryCleared`(full-delete sync) handlers on the client. Previously the server did not handle `DeleteChannelHistory` → **🗑 permanent-delete was not persisted server-side, resurrecting on refresh + unsynced across multi-browser boards** (this fix resolves both the persistence bug + cross-board sync). **(4) routing-independent early handling of `SelectionResolved`** — handled at the top of onWsEvent (before the agent-outbound agentId guard) so the chip dims even when arriving as a direct server reply without agentId (previously only inside the agent-outbound switch → required passing the agentId guard, a defensive-coverage gap). **(5) 4-role color tint on member tab names when a group is selected** — `wsRenderTabs` adds `grpSel = (active===group)` + assigns the group cls to `.nm` + CSS `.ws-tab .nm.{up,main,local,collab}` 4 roles (previously `.ws-tab.up/.main .nm` 2-role always-on color → 4-role tint on group selection). **Files modified**: Constellation.md(frontmatter v2.4.7 → v2.4.8 + codicil); plugins/constellation/.claude-plugin/plugin.json(v0.3.7 → v0.3.8 + desc); constellation/reference/dashboard/app.js(wsMsgEpoch/wsRowTime + unified _t/_ts + badge hidden + early SelectionResolved + grpSel + DeleteChannelHistory/HistoryCleared handlers) + dashboard/style.css(.nm 4-role); constellation/reference/runtime/server.cjs(DeleteChannelHistory handler); README(badge + Current/현재 EN+KO); docs/index.html(hero badge v2.5.67 → v2.5.68 + module-tag v2.4.7 → v2.4.8); docs/shared/data.js(v2.5.67 → v2.5.68 + shipCount 83 → 84); .claude-plugin/marketplace.json(metadata 0.3.13 → 0.3.14 + constellation v0.3.7 → v0.3.8); CHANGELOG. **Module versions**: Constellation v2.4.7 → **v2.4.8**(patch — dashboard parity + server DeleteChannelHistory handler, no wire change: adds server-side handling + board broadcast for an existing client→server message, no impact on non-handling adopters), plugin v0.3.7 → v0.3.8. - **v2.5.67** (2026-06-07) — **Constellation v2.4.7 single-workspace multi-agent session-aware routing (register-all + fail-safe) + dashboard issuance bug fix** — when multiple Claude Code sessions (main + local worker, etc.) are open in the same workspace, they share-execute the same Stop hook (`pre-send-probe --rearm`) → contention on the same A2A cursor (a worker turn-end advances main's surfacing cursor first → main never sees the inbound; surface theft). Avoids splitting into separate workspaces (duplicate extension loading per IDE window + harness/doc context severance cost) by branching on the **per-session env `CLAUDE_CODE_SESSION_ID`** (injected into the hook process by Claude Code — `src=env` empirically confirmed, stdin payload `.session_id` fallback). **register-all model**: every session (main included) declares its own inboxes in the `<cwd>/.agent-sessions.json` registry; each hook run processes only SELF-owned inboxes — (a) unregistered/unidentifiable session → SKIP-ALL (fail-safe: no cursor advance, never intrudes on another session's surface — main protection guaranteed by mechanism, not discipline), (b) inbox owned by another session → skip, (c) ownerless inbox → skip (register-all requires explicit ownership), (d) self-owned → normal processing. When the registry is inactive (absent/empty workers), legacy default (single-session workspace, identical to before) — back-compat. **New/changed files**: `runtime/stop-hook/register-session.cjs` (NEW — registers/validates/releases session `{role, ownInboxes}`, keyed by `CLAUDE_CODE_SESSION_ID`) + `runtime/stop-hook/pre-send-probe.cjs` (register-all routing block — 6/6 case simulation PASS) + `runtime/scripts/join-local.cjs` v2.4.7 (local worker `OUTBOX` drain = the worker session appends to the outbox file → join-local sends via a 1.5s drain, new worker emit path + full inbound logging so Delegate value bodies are read) + `runtime/server.cjs` (startup warning when WS_PRIMARY_AGENT is unset — when unset, the main session is demoted to local; mechanizes `feedback_self_board_restart_env`). **Two-tier wakeup for low-latency A2A inbox reception**: tier 1 = ≤5s polling file Monitor (immediate wakeup on event), tier 2 = long ScheduleWakeup fallback heartbeat (1200-1800s) — relying on ScheduleWakeup cadence (minute-scale) alone delays reception by that much (confirmed by the 2026-06-07 case where board-observer waited for a Delegate until the /loop cadence). **Dashboard issuance bug fix (Cut A bundle)**: blocked the `.ws-collab-*` cursor:move leak (`.ws-pop-head`'s cursor:move was inherited down the issuance panel's child chain — leak path confirmed via Playwright) + (private self-board) 5-handler drift fix for KEY-MGMT responses (root cause of key issuance stalling at "발급 중…" — the outer dashboard was missing the v2.4.0 canonical KeyIssued/KeyError/KeyListResult/KeyRevoked·Labeled·RevokePending handlers, confirmed via Playwright WS frame capture). **Live verification**: round-trip with the local worker (board-observer) — Delegate→WorkerAck/WorkerReport, **direct proof of main-cursor non-collision** (multiple worker turn-ends SKIP the collab-self inbox → main cursor held at 287; the worker's 3 replies remained unsurfaced and main's next hook surfaced them normally) + main auto-reception (≤3s file Monitor, no nudge). **Files modified**: Constellation.md(frontmatter v2.4.6 → v2.4.7 + codicil); plugins/constellation/.claude-plugin/plugin.json(v0.3.6 → v0.3.7); pre-send-probe.cjs + register-session.cjs(NEW) + scripts/join-local.cjs + server.cjs + dashboard/style.css; README(badge + Current/현재 EN+KO); docs/index.html(hero badge v2.5.66 → v2.5.67 + module-tag v2.4.6 → v2.4.7); docs/shared/data.js(v2.5.66 → v2.5.67 + shipCount 82 → 83); .claude-plugin/marketplace.json(metadata 0.3.12 → 0.3.13 + constellation v0.3.6 → v0.3.7); CHANGELOG. **Module versions**: Constellation v2.4.6 → **v2.4.7**(patch — register-all routing + dashboard fix, no wire change), plugin v0.3.6 → v0.3.7. Other modules unchanged(Superscalar v0.4.2 · Hyperbrief v0.6.0 · Greatpractice v0.2.0 · Ultrasafe v0.2.0). Section contains: 4-case classification table (1:1 A2A · user-visible progress · system event · uncertain → A2A main fallback), 4 recommended rules (first message after join · progress reports · user-visible intent · multi-recipient loop), and 3 anti-patterns (missing `targetAgentId` → server fallback to main inbox shows in user tab unintentionally; arbitrary board broadcast attempt; direct `state.json` mutation by non-main agent). Discovered from observation that joining agents routinely emit `targetAgentId`-less CUSTOM frames that land in main's tab, conflating "1:1 with main" intent with "broadcast to user" effect. Two spec corrections added to candidate #7 (tone-axis term-pairing) from user input: **(a) structural exclusion of the C (conversation) scope** — the C scope is unaffected by all three retroactive_apply options prompt/Y/N (rewriting the author's own historical output is difficult + determinism is hard to guarantee + cognitive load + negligible consistency value; the command `L1.I.C` → apply immediately without asking; `L1.I.C+D` → prompt for the D portion only). **(b) low-frequency override for I (initial) mode** — when a term is used ≤ 3 times within the application-scope unit, pair it on every occurrence even in I mode; from 4 uses and up, spell out only the first mention (rationale: author cognitive load + the longer the gap, the harder abbreviation recall + accounting for the distance across Hyperbrief brief's 9 sections × multiple items). - **v2.5.44** (2026-06-04) — **`constellation/reference/runtime/stop-hook/pre-send-probe.cjs` self-emission echo filter — drop lines where `o.ev === "sent"` during meaningful classification. The bridge logs both outbound (`ev:"sent"`) and inbound (`ev:"inbound"`) to the same inbox.log file, so without this gate the §13.16.9 name-only allowlist (Report / Delegate / WorkerReport / Request / PRRequest / etc.) classified every outbox push as meaningful inbound on the next probe — a self-emission echo class that polluted the watch-state cycle.** Watch-state hygiene patch cut. Diagnosis: v2.4.16 (3565b32) removed a `grep '"ev":"in...'` 1st-stage gate because some adopter bridges write inbound without the `ev` marker; the removal correctly unblocked bridge-alive direct inbound, but it implicitly admitted self-emission `ev:"sent"` lines into the classification pipeline. The downstream §13.16.9 allowlist filters by message name only, so every outbound A2A-intent push (Report, Delegate, PRRequest, etc.) re-appeared as meaningful inbound on the next Stop hook fire — the agent's `feedback_pre_send_inbound_check.md` discipline then forced a "read meaningful body + classify" round-trip that costs context without supplying any new information, since the body was the agent's own just-sent payload. Real observed incident: after EG outbox push 348 (`m-eg-cycle1-ack-1780528600` Report to main), the next Stop hook surface listed line 23271 as meaningful — the very same Report content the agent had just composed. **Fix**: `if (o?.ev === 'sent') continue;` injected immediately after the `JSON.parse` step in `probe()` (lines 90-91 area). Per-line `ev:"sent"` SKIP, NOT an `ev:"inbound"` REQUIRE — adopters whose bridges write inbound without the `ev` marker continue to have their inbound surfaced normally (the v2.4.16 regression risk is preserved). Inline comment block documents the design choice + cross-references v2.4.16 + v2.5.20 doubly-wrapped envelope handling (orthogonal — `value.name` fallback still applies after the self-emission skip). **No protocol wire change** — this is a Stop hook reference-impl classification fix, not a §13.x specification change. No `Constellation.md` body change. No `local-bridge.eux` change. No `Hyperbrief.md` change. No plugin manifest change. No schema change. No renderer change. No seed lib change. **docs/promo catch-up**: `docs/index.html` hero badge `v2.5.43 → v2.5.44`; `docs/shared/data.js` meta `'v2.5.43' → 'v2.5.44'` + `shipCount: 59 → 60`; `README.md` top badge `v2.5.43 → v2.5.44` + `Current:` line rewritten (EN + KO) to describe the self-emission echo gap + fix + the v2.5.43/v2.5.42/v2.5.44 patch arc. **Scope discipline**: `constellation/reference/runtime/stop-hook/pre-send-probe.cjs` (~10 lines net change: 1 skip line + comment block) + `CHANGELOG.md` (this entry, EN + KO) + `docs/index.html` hero badge + `docs/shared/data.js` meta + `README.md` top badge + Versioning Current line (EN + KO). - **v2.5.43** (2026-06-04) — **`constellation/reference/runtime/local-bridge.cjs` outboxCursor init aligned with `local-bridge.eux` `@state.outboxCursor` spec (init = EOF, pre-existing lines skipped on respawn). Closes a spec-vs-impl mismatch where the implementation initialized `outboxCursor = 0` at module init, causing the entire accumulated outbox.jsonl to be re-shipped on every bridge restart — §13.13.2 server-side dedup masked the application-level impact (every duplicate carried the same `msgId` and was rejected with `AckProcessed{dedupHit:true}`), but bandwidth + log noise was significant: a 19h disconnection window followed by respawn replayed 331 `ev:'sent'` entries in a single drain cycle in a real observed incident.** Bridge runtime patch cut. The `local-bridge.eux` `@state.outboxCursor` declaration documents the intended behavior as `byte offset already shipped from outbox (init = EOF so pre-existing lines are skipped)`, and `derive.connected_gate` reiterates `cursor inits at EOF`. The reference C implementation in `local-bridge.cjs` however set `let outboxCursor = 0;` at module init, then byte-offset-tailed from there — diverging from the spec by treating all pre-existing outbox content as un-shipped on every spawn. Adopters using the reference impl experienced the same backlog-replay behavior on every bridge restart; `feedback_a2a_relay_reliability.md`'s at-most-once relay note further compounds the concern (transport-tier `Ack delivered` does not guarantee recipient inbox has the body, but here the wire was carrying re-sends of already-acknowledged content). **Fix**: replaces `let outboxCursor = 0;` with `function initOutboxCursor() { try { return fs.statSync(OUTBOX).size; } catch { return 0; } } let outboxCursor = initOutboxCursor();` — module-init reads the current outbox.jsonl file size and treats that as the cursor's starting position. Pre-existing lines are now skipped per the spec. Inline comment block updated to call out the alignment and reference the §13.13.2 dedup masking that hid the impact previously. **Trade-off discipline**: this matches spec intent but means lines appended to outbox.jsonl while the bridge is dead will be lost on respawn. The spec assumes the agent only appends when the bridge is live; adopters needing queue-during-restart semantics can override (e.g., persist cursor across restarts) as an opt-in extension — recommended pattern documented in the inline comment. EG's own outer `EstreGenesis-maintenance` workspace runs a separate `collab/collab-client.cjs` with line-count-based cursor persistence as a stricter local choice; that file is not part of the public reference impl. **No protocol wire change** — this is a reference impl alignment, not a §13.x specification change. No `Constellation.md` body change. No `local-bridge.eux` change (spec already documented the correct behavior). No `local-bridge-and-watcher-NOTES.md` change (the bug was in `.cjs`, not in the spec NOTES). No plugin manifest change. No schema change. No renderer change. No seed lib change. **docs/promo catch-up**: `docs/index.html` hero badge `v2.5.42 → v2.5.43`; `docs/shared/data.js` meta `'v2.5.42' → 'v2.5.43'` + `shipCount: 58 → 59`; `README.md` top badge `v2.5.42 → v2.5.43` + `Current:` line rewritten (EN + KO) to describe the bridge fix + §13.13.2 dedup masking. **Scope discipline**: `constellation/reference/runtime/local-bridge.cjs` (~4 lines net change) + `CHANGELOG.md` (this entry, EN + KO) + `docs/index.html` hero badge + `docs/shared/data.js` meta + `README.md` top badge + Versioning Current line (EN + KO). Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` — bridge reference-impl bug fix surfaced by an adopter-equivalent incident is a meaningful push, cut as a patch release. Per `feedback_public_repo_redaction.md` — no chat verbatim, no governance attribution; the trade-off rationale stays technical.

- **v2.5.41** (2026-06-03) — **Hyperbrief v0.5.5 → v0.5.6 — §5.6.7 tone-floor fallback auto-localize discipline codified (skill MUST populate `audience_profile_fallback.button_label` AND `audience_profile_fallback.trigger_phrases_md` in the user's prevailing conversation language at IR-emit time; schema/renderer Korean defaults demoted to last-resort fallback for IR-direct-call/test only; reference EN/KO/JA literals + trigger lists named in §5.6.7 and SKILL.md). MUST-19 rewritten to fold the discipline in normatively. docs/promo Hyperbrief card (`docs/index.html`) + overview (`docs/hyperbrief.html`) general-tier prose updated to show both EN and KO button literals side-by-side with a "follows the user's language" / "사용자 언어에 따름" parenthetical.** Same-day design correction cut. User flagged that the v2.5.40 promo prose `"(canonical EG default localizes to plain Korean; adopters localize)"` reflected a real design problem — the schema default `button_label` is hardcoded Korean (`"뭔 소리야? 한국어로 번역해줘 (내가 알아들을 수 있는 말로)"`) and `trigger_phrases_md` default is Korean-only, with the v0.5.0 spec saying "adopters localize for non-Korean reader-bases SHOULD". This conflated *EG-the-project* (Korean) with *Hyperbrief-the-library* (a public module that ships to adopters in any language); the practical reality is that the skill (LLM composing the IR) already knows the user's prevailing conversation language and can populate the IR accordingly, so the schema's Korean default never needs to surface for non-Korean users in normal flow. The fix is skill-side discipline (not schema change → deterministic invariant preserved). **§5.6.7 HTML surface bullet** rewritten as two bullets: the first names the permanent re-render button + the `audience_profile_fallback.button_label` slot; the second is a new **Auto-localization at IR-emit time (v0.5.6 — load-bearing default)** bullet that mandates skill-side population in the user's prevailing conversation language, names reference literals for EN (`"What? Just say it plainly."`) / KO (`"뭔 소리야? 한국어로 번역해줘 (내가 알아들을 수 있는 말로)"`) / JA (`"何これ？私が分かる言葉で。"`), specifies mixed-language session handling (follow most recent prevailing-language signal), and clarifies that schema/renderer defaults are last-resort fallback for IR-direct-call / programmatic / test invocations only — in normal skill-driven flow this fallback never surfaces. Same auto-localize discipline applies to `trigger_phrases_md` (skill populates the trigger list in the user's prevailing language). Hard override at `.hyperbrief/profile.json` takes precedence for adopters who want a fixed single language. **§5.6.7 MD surface bullet** updated to reference the auto-localized trigger list from the new discipline. **MUST-19** rewritten to fold the auto-localize discipline in as normative: skill MUST populate both `button_label` and `trigger_phrases_md` in the user's language at IR-emit time; schema defaults are last-resort fallback only; in skill-driven flow the Korean fallback MUST NOT surface for non-Korean users. **`plugins/hyperbrief/skills/hyperbrief/SKILL.md`** — section 1 table's `audience_profile_fallback` row extended with explicit reference EN/KO/JA literals + trigger lists (EN: `what?`, `huh?`, `say it plainly`, `i don't get it`, `too much jargon`, `try again simpler`, `in plain english`, `eli5`; KO: `뭔 소리`, `안 읽혀`, `무슨 말`, `이해 안`, `더 쉽게`, `너무 어렵`, `다시 풀어`, `쉽게 다시`, `한국어로`, `한국말로`; analogous JA) + mixed-language session handling + hard override precedence note. **No schema change** — the schema `default` for `button_label` and `trigger_phrases_md` stays Korean (load-bearing for IR-direct-call test invocations and for backwards compatibility with v0.5.0-v0.5.5 IRs that omit the fields); the discipline is enforced at the skill layer (LLM composing the IR), which is the natural place since the LLM knows the user's language and the renderer does not. **No renderer change** — the renderer's fallback to the schema default stays (`mini-engine.cjs:414`); the discipline shifts WHERE the populated value comes from, not WHAT the renderer does. **Determinism invariant preserved** — same IR + same options → same output bytes (the auto-localize happens upstream at IR-compose time; the IR itself still uniquely determines the surface). **docs/promo updates**: `docs/index.html` Hyperbrief card general-tier prose rewritten — EN: `"...in plain language you can parse with a single click — the button reads \"What? Just say it plainly.\" in English, \"뭔 소리야? 한국어로 번역해줘\" in Korean (follows the user's language)"`; KO: `"...한 번의 버튼 클릭으로 평이한 언어로 다시 풀어쓰게 할 수도 있어요 — 버튼 문구는 한국어 「뭔 소리야? 한국어로 번역해줘」, 영어 「What? Just say it plainly.」 (사용자 언어에 따름)"`. `docs/hyperbrief.html` general-tier overview prose updated analogously. dev/expert-tier prose unchanged (they already described the affordance abstractly without language-hardcoding). **Hyperbrief frontmatter** `version: v0.5.5 → v0.5.6` + status string rewritten to reflect the auto-localize discipline + reference literals + SKILL.md update. **§11.1 v0.5.6 entry** new (inserted at the top of the v0.5.x sequence): records the §5.6.7 + MUST-19 rewrite + SKILL.md update + the design-conflation closure rationale (EG-project vs Hyperbrief-library layer separation). **Plugin manifest + sibling package.json** all bump `0.5.5 → 0.5.6` (plugin / renderers / mcp). **docs/promo catch-up**: hero badges `v0.5.5 → v0.5.6`; meta description gains the auto-localize clause; `docs/index.html` hero EG version `v2.5.40 → v2.5.41` + Hyperbrief badge `v0.5.5 → v0.5.6` + card module-tag `v0.5.5 → v0.5.6`; `docs/shared/data.js` meta `'v2.5.40' → 'v2.5.41'` + `shipCount: 56 → 57`. **Scope discipline**: `Hyperbrief.md` body (§5.6.7 + MUST-19 + §11.1 v0.5.6 entry + frontmatter version) + `plugins/hyperbrief/skills/hyperbrief/SKILL.md` (section 1 table `audience_profile_fallback` row) + 3 package.json version bumps + docs/promo (`docs/index.html` Hyperbrief card general-tier + hero badges + module-tag + `docs/hyperbrief.html` general-tier overview + hero badge + meta + `docs/shared/data.js` meta). - **v2.5.40** (2026-06-03) — **Hyperbrief v0.5.4 → v0.5.5 — §11.5 v1.0 readiness rubric codified (two evaluation lenses: Lens A 7-dim module-wide GA / Lens B 6-dim host-specific marketplace registration). dogfood Entry 04 archived: Claude plugin marketplace registration decision — `defer to v1.0 GA` (`one_way_with_migration_path` 🟡, decided 2026-06-03). docs/promo hyperbrief.html now carries the same `Want to read more? → Read the full spec → github.com/.../Hyperbrief.md →` section the other two module promo pages have carried since v2.5.16.** Decision-methodology codify cut. The user asked whether to register Hyperbrief now in the Anthropic Claude plugin marketplace; the brief surfaced four alternatives (immediate community submission / wait until v1.0 GA / EG-only fork-and-clone / hybrid double-track). User critique R3 — *"v1.0 라는 라벨 자체가 자의적이라, 그 기준을 먼저 세우는 게 우선"* — surfaced that the v1.0 label is maintainer-discretion and needs an explicit anchored rubric BEFORE the marketplace decision can be made meaningfully. User critique R4 — *"Claude marketplace 등록 판단 평가에서는 cross-host portability 차원 제외"* — surfaced that the rubric needs lens-splitting (module-wide GA vs host-specific registration). The cut codifies BOTH critiques into Hyperbrief.md §11.5 as a reusable methodology. **§11.5 v1.0 readiness rubric** new sub-section (~70 lines, inserted between §11.4 host self-config gate and the §11 closing) carries: (a) **Lens A** — 7 dimensions for module-wide GA `Spec completeness / Schema stability / External adopter validation / Emergency-fix cadence settled / Cross-host portability / Docs maturity / Determinism guarantee` with 0/5/10 scoring anchors per dimension; (b) **Lens B** — 6 dimensions for Claude-host-specific marketplace registration (drops Cross-host portability since it's logically orthogonal to a single-host registration decision); (c) **Aggregation** — simple mean + weighted mean (default weights: Emergency-fix cadence ×2.0; Schema stability / External adopter validation / Determinism guarantee ×1.5; others ×1.0); (d) **Thresholds** — Lens A ≥ 8.0 weighted mean for v1.0 cut; Lens B ≥ 7.5 weighted mean for marketplace registration; (e) **Current scoring at v0.5.5** — Lens A 5.3 simple / 4.9 weighted; Lens B 5.5 simple / 5.1 weighted; both sub-threshold; (f) **Gap analysis** — binding constraints converge on Emergency-fix cadence (currently 2/10, time-bound — first 30-day no-emergency-fix baseline is the only way) + External adopter validation (currently 3/10 — EstreUF dogfood Entry 01 + at least one more adopter is the short-term lift); (g) **Re-evaluation cadence** — re-score on ≥2-pt move on any single dimension OR emergency-fix release OR explicit decision-point trigger; first scheduled review 2026-09-01. **Marketplace decision outcome**: `defer to v1.0 GA + codify §11.5 rubric` (the codified methodology is the load-bearing artifact, not the decision itself — future maturity-claim decisions (EstreUF v1.0, other modules' marketplace registration) all consume the same rubric for cross-project consistency). **dogfood Entry 04 archive** at `_proposals/006_2026-06-03_hyperbrief/dogfood-entry-04.md` per §9 `archive_config` (default ON): 5-element bundle (brief_original.md including R1→R2→R3→R4 four-step tone+methodology boost / decision.json with 4 agent_judgment_calls including the two-lens split decision + default-weight choice / related_user_prompts.md with R1 AF-22 Korean fallback + R3 arbitrariness critique + R4 lens-split critique / recommended_artifacts_applied.md detailing 6 artifacts including the §11.5 new sub-section + Entry 04 archive itself + plugin manifest bumps / meta_learnings.md surfacing 3 new schema gap candidates: (1) `recommended_methodology[]` slot — schema should carry the *decision methodology itself* alongside per-decision artifacts; (2) `evaluation_lens` field — schema should model multiple-lens scoring of the same decision target; (3) `maturity_anchor` field — schema should require anchored criteria when the IR uses arbitrary labels like "v1.0" / "production-ready" / "GA" / "stable"). This is the first dogfood entry where the load-bearing output is a *reusable methodology* (the rubric itself) rather than a single decision — Entries 01-03 all archived single decisions; Entry 04 archives both a decision AND the methodology that produced it. **§11.1 v0.5.5 entry** new (inserted at the top of the v0.5.x sequence): records §11.5 codification + Entry 04 archive + marketplace deferral. **§11.2 dogfood ledger** recent-3-row index updated to include Entry 04 as the new top row; external `_proposals/006/dogfood-ledger.md` Recent table also extended with Entry 04 row. **Hyperbrief frontmatter** `version: v0.5.4 → v0.5.5` + status string rewritten to reflect Entry 04 archive + §11.5 rubric codify + marketplace deferral decision. **Plugin manifest + sibling package.json** all bump `0.5.4 → 0.5.5` (plugin / renderers / mcp). **`docs/promo` catch-up** — `docs/hyperbrief.html` gains the same `Want to read more? → Read the full spec → github.com/SoliEstre/EstreGenesis/blob/main/Hyperbrief.md →` section the other two module promo pages have carried since v2.5.16 (parity restored — Hyperbrief page was the only one without the explicit spec-link section); hero badge `v0.5.4 → v0.5.5` + new `v1.0 readiness rubric (§11.5)` badge + `3 dogfood + 2 adopter reports → 4 dogfood + 2 adopter reports`; meta description gains the §11.5 two-lens rubric clause; `docs/index.html` Hyperbrief card module-tag `v0.5.4 → v0.5.5` + hero badges `Hyperbrief v0.5.4 → v0.5.5` + EG version `v2.5.38 → v2.5.40`; `docs/shared/data.js` meta `'v2.5.38' → 'v2.5.40'` + `shipCount: 54 → 56`. **Scope discipline**: `Hyperbrief.md` body (§11.5 new sub-section + §11.1 v0.5.5 entry + §11.2 recent-3 index row + frontmatter version) + 3 package.json version bumps + `_proposals/006_2026-06-03_hyperbrief/dogfood-entry-04.md` new + `_proposals/006_2026-06-03_hyperbrief/dogfood-ledger.md` row added + docs/promo (hyperbrief.html new section + hero badges + meta + index.html card + data.js). The adopter caught this by running clean-install ajv 8.x + validation-on, exactly the same regression-vector as H1; this time they chose pure-mirror-plus-`--skip-validate` over vendor-patch (the M3 trade-off learning paid off — vendor patches against a 1-hour-turnaround upstream become redundant before they ship). **H7 fix** — both `renderMd` (line ~328) and `renderHtml` (line ~383) reordered: (1) `stampRecommendedArtifacts(ir)` stays first because the stamped fields (line_count + body_hash) are part of the IR contract and travel with archive bundles, schema-valid by construction; (2) `validateIr(ir)` now runs on the canonical IR (tag prefix intact) — schema passes; (3) `const renderIr = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(ir))` deep-clones for rendering only; (4) `stripHeadingEpistemicTag(renderIr)` mutates the clone (IR original preserved); (5) `substitute(template, renderIr, surface)` uses the cloned IR. In `renderHtml`, the inline `IR_JSON` placeholder is also fed the stripped clone so the embedded debug-IR agrees with the surface — `archive_config` callers pass the original `ir` separately to maintain audit invariance. Net code change: ~6 lines added per entrypoint + comment block explaining the fix. **Smoke test PASS** — clean ajv 8.x environment, full FullBrief IR with all sections populated, validation-on default path: MD render PASS (hash `c5e4ef58aa2edf3f`, 2 warnings — AF-18 audience-profile-estimate gap, expected), HTML render PASS (hash `2afe182dfdf65b15`); IR original `essence_one_line` confirmed to still start with `[verified]` post-render (pre-v0.5.4 would have crashed before the assertion ran). **§11.3 vendor-patch-vs-pure-mirror trade-off** — new paragraph at the end of §11.3 (`Cross-seed adoption`) codifying the M3 / H1-vs-H7 learning: vendor patch is the right call when upstream turnaround is slow; pure-mirror-plus-workaround is the right call when upstream turnaround is fast (like the EG-owner-as-adopter ~1h baseline measured in bundle 008 002). Either way, the choice should be EXPLICIT in the adopter's project notes so future contributors know whether the local diff is intentional drift or a temporary workaround. **§11.4 host self-config approval gate** — new paragraph at the end of §11.4 (`Hook-tier review queue`) covering the adopter-installation reality: registering the hook with the running Claude Code session requires editing `.claude/settings.json` (or equivalent), which the host's auto-mode classifier treats as agent-runtime self-modification and blocks without explicit user approval.
