- **v2.5.37** (2026-06-03) — **Hyperbrief v0.5.2 → v0.5.3 — PreToolUse + Stop hooks activated in advise mode (closes the Phase 2 PreToolUse-hook item carried as "deferred" since v0.4.0) + new review-queue routing extending the simple alert into a deferred-review pipeline (Constellation-on → DECISION_REQUEST envelope to board; Constellation-off + auto_generate_review_doc=on → `.hyperbrief/pending-reviews/<id>.md` placeholder; default 'ask' → stderr advise + setup hint; off → simple alert). New `Hyperbrief.md §11.4` codifies the hook-tier discipline as plugin-tier (Claude Code-specific) on top of the host-agnostic SSoT-tier `SKILL.md` model-invoked discipline. dogfood Entry 03 archived.** Hook activation cut. The v0.4.0 status entry had carried "PreToolUse hook + MCP server **deferred to v0.4.1+**"; the MCP server landed at v0.4.2 (cut v2.5.28), but the PreToolUse hook stayed in the `hooks.json` Phase 1 placeholder through v0.5.0 → v0.5.1 → v0.5.2 as each cycle prioritized schema / cross-module integration / clean-install blocker fixes. v2.5.37 closes the carry with an advise-mode hook design (exit 0, never block) that adds a *silent-skip detection layer* over the existing model-invoked SKILL.md discipline. **Hook architecture** — three files under `plugins/hyperbrief/hooks/`: (1) `hooks.json` — Claude Code hook registration (PreToolUse `AskUserQuestion` + `Bash` + Stop `*`); (2) `trigger-advise.cjs` (~190 LoC, deps-0 except Node stdlib) — the PreToolUse wrapper, runs on every matching tool call with stdin = tool input JSON, applies the danger-list match for Bash (12 patterns: `git push` / `gh release` / `gh pr create|merge` / `npm publish` / `pnpm publish` / `yarn publish` / `kubectl apply|delete|create` / `docker push` / `terraform apply` / `gcloud …deploy` / `aws s3 cp|sync|update|deploy` / `curl -X POST|PUT|DELETE`), generates a `decision_id` matching the §1 pattern, then routes per the 4-way decision tree (Constellation detection + standalone preference); (3) `revisit-scan.cjs` (~85 LoC) — the Stop wrapper, scans `hyperbrief-ledger.jsonl` for `revisit_date ≤ today` (excluding rows with `outcome_actual` filled) and `.hyperbrief/pending-reviews/` for unreviewed placeholders, emits a single advisory line on either signal. **Review-queue routing** (the user-requested extension): on PreToolUse hook fire, the script detects whether Constellation is reachable (CONSTELLATION_WS_URL env set + a local outbox path exists at one of `$CONSTELLATION_OUTBOX_PATH`, `assets/collab/outbox.jsonl`, or `.constellation/outbox.jsonl`). If yes → append a `DECISION_REQUEST` envelope to the outbox as a *pending-review placeholder* (carries `decision_id`, `origin: "hyperbrief-hook"`, `pending: true`, `detected_tool`, `detected_intent`, `stage: "pending-review"`, `ack_tier_required: "decided"`); the local Constellation bridge relays the envelope to the board and the board's decisions/review-items panel surfaces it; stderr advise mentions the board surface explicitly. If no → check `auto_generate_review_doc` (env `HYPERBRIEF_AUTO_GENERATE_REVIEW_DOC=on|off|ask` or `.hyperbrief/config.json {auto_generate_review_doc: "on"|"off"|"ask"}`, default `"ask"`). When `"on"` → write a placeholder MD to `.hyperbrief/pending-reviews/<decision_id>.md` carrying detected tool + intent + raw tool input clipped to 4KB + next-step instructions; stderr advise mentions the file path. When `"ask"` (default) → stderr advise only + setup-hint pointing at the config knob. When `"off"` → simple stderr alert, no file. This 4-way design lets the hook function as a *deferred-review pipeline* — the user can defer decisions for later inspection rather than being forced into immediate-or-skip dichotomy at the alert moment, which composes cleanly with the §2.4 alert-fatigue circuit breaker. The pending → HyperbriefCard upgrade follows the same envelope-pair pattern Constellation §13.16.9 already carries (DECISION_REQUEST + paired HyperbriefCard by parentId; ack_tier='decided' on the Constellation MCP `a2a_wait_ack` side per v2.5.28). **`Hyperbrief.md §11.4` Hook-tier review queue (v0.5.3 — Claude Code plugin-tier discipline)** new sub-section ~60 lines: hook contract (advise mode invariants); 4-way review-queue routing with stderr message templates; "why advise mode (not hard-block)" rationale grounded in §2.4 alert-fatigue circuit breaker semantics; falsification triggers (10/day → matcher too broad; 0/week with samples accumulating → matcher too narrow or stderr propagation broken; 3+ revisits past date → notify-on-revisit opt-in candidate); cross-references to Constellation §13.16.9 / §13.16.10 + Hyperbrief §8. The sub-section explicitly names the hook layer as **plugin-tier (Claude Code-specific)** to preserve cross-host SSoT portability — Codex / Cursor / other hosts continue to rely on the model-invoked SKILL.md description discipline alone, and the SSoT-tier rules in §1–§10 remain identical across hosts. **`Hyperbrief.md §11.1` v0.5.3 entry** new (inserted before the v0.5.0 entry): explicitly records "Closes the Phase 2 PreToolUse-hook item from the v0.4.0 status entry" + names the 4-way routing decision tree. **dogfood Entry 03 archive** at `_proposals/006_2026-06-03_hyperbrief/dogfood-entry-03.md` per §9 `archive_config` (default ON): 5-element bundle (brief_original.md including R1 → R2 tone fallback cycle / decision.json with 3 agent_judgment_calls including the user-requested extension / related_user_prompts.md with the §5.6.7 fallback trigger utterance "음....역시 한국어로 부탁해" + the user-requested 4-way extension prompt / recommended_artifacts_applied.md detailing the 5 artifacts (hooks.json activation + trigger-advise.cjs ~190 LoC + revisit-scan.cjs ~85 LoC + §11.4 new sub-section + §11.1 v0.5.3 entry) / meta_learnings.md surfacing 2 new schema/operational gaps: (1) `surface_profile_estimate` heuristic's technical-domain false-negative — the v0.5 declared-vs-effective gap warning AF-18 should have fired on R1 but didn't because the `english_noun_ratio` heuristic includes code-block + identifier-quotation tokens; v0.6 candidate patch = exclude fenced code blocks; (2) `trigger_phrases_md` `한국어로` pattern matched at v2.5.30 default-set inclusion BUT model-self-invoke without hook-tier reinforcement still missed the auto-regen — this very cycle is the self-evidencing case for why the hook activation is justified). **§11.2 dogfood ledger** recent-3-row index updated to include Entry 03 as the new top row + Constellation/Superscalar cross-references unchanged; external `_proposals/006/dogfood-ledger.md` Recent table also extended with Entry 03 row. **Hyperbrief frontmatter** `version: v0.5.2 → v0.5.3` + status string rewritten to flag the dogfood Entry 03 close of the v0.4.0 deferred PreToolUse-hook item. **Plugin manifest + sibling package.json** all bump `0.5.2 → 0.5.3` (plugin / renderers / mcp). **Smoke test PASS**: `node --check` on both wrapper scripts; - **v2.5.35** (2026-06-03) — **Seed lib v2.4.1 → v2.4.2 — Migration B dual-track guidance per bundle 007 M1: Step 1 (Identify starting version) + Step 2 (Diff capabilities) now explicitly describe the seed-version vs EG-release-version separation and require cross-checking BOTH markers before declaring a starting state. Cascades across all 6 seed tiers (Master + Lite + Compact × EN/KO).** Seed-lib cut. Bundle 007 M1 surfaced a 2-track tracking gap: the seed-version marker (e.g., `v2.4.1`, embedded in `AGENTS.md`) and the EG-release version (e.g., `v2.5.x`, advancing on every meaningful push per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md`) are independent — a release-only cut (e.g., Constellation `§13.x` patch, Hyperbrief module ship) does NOT bump the seed version, so a migrating adopter that checks only the seed marker may conclude "no delta" when substantial module/spec changes have landed. The fix is a Migration B Step 1 + Step 2 rewrite (Master tier full, Lite tier condensed, Compact tier 1-liner) that makes the dual-track expectation explicit. **Master tier (Master EN + Master KO)** — Step 1 expanded from one paragraph to a structured sub-section naming the two tracks ("seed version" vs "EG release version") + a "Check both markers before declaring a starting version" paragraph explaining the failure mode + cross-check sources (AGENTS.md seed marker + adoption manifest EG-release + upstream `CHANGELOG.md` HEAD) + revised user-question wording ("which EG release tag was current at that time?"). Step 2 prefaced with "List X for the starting **seed version** (table below), AND list Y for the starting **release version** (consult upstream `CHANGELOG.md` between the two release tags — typically a `git log <starting-tag>..HEAD --oneline -- CHANGELOG.md` against the EG repo, or just read the CHANGELOG entries between the two tags)" and the existing seed-delta table is now labeled "Seed-delta table" so readers know it's only one of the two tracks. **Lite tier (Lite EN + Lite KO)** — condensed equivalent: Step 1 carries the dual-track explanation in 2 sentences + cross-check instruction; Step 2 prefaced with the dual-track diff. **Compact tier (Compact EN + Compact KO)** — 1-liner extension at the start of Step 1 + 1-liner reframe of Step 2 ("diff capabilities (both tracks)"). **Frontmatter version markers** — all 6 tier headers bump `version: v2.4.1 → v2.4.2` + `date: 2026-05-31 → 2026-06-03` + status fragment `v2.4.2 = bundle 007 M1 reflection — Migration B Step 1/2 dual-track guidance` (Master) / condensed forms (Lite + Compact). **Why a seed bump (rather than just a CHANGELOG note)** — the change is to the seed body itself (Migration B procedure), not to a referenced module — adopters bootstrapping new projects from this seed cut get the dual-track guidance built into the Migration B section, not as an out-of-band CHANGELOG cross-reference. The seed-version marker was unchanged since v2.4.1 (2026-05-31) because the prior cuts (v2.5.0 through v2.5.34) were all release-track changes that did not touch the seed body — this is the first true seed-body change since v2.4.1, validating the 2-track separation that the change itself codifies. **Cross-tier consistency check passes** — the dual-track guidance is now present in all 6 tiers; the substance is identical (two tracks, cross-check both, ask user which EG release tag was current); the verbosity scales per tier (Master = full prose explanation, Lite = 2 sentences, Compact = 1 line). **Scope discipline**: 6 seed-tier files (Master EN + Master KO + Lite EN + Lite KO + Compact EN + Compact KO) — each gets Migration B Step 1 and Step 2 prefix updates + frontmatter version bump. No module changes (Constellation.md / Superscalar.md / Hyperbrief.md untouched). No plugin changes. No reference runtime changes. No schema changes. No renderer changes. No docs/promo changes. No wire format changes. - **v2.5.34** (2026-06-03) — **Hyperbrief v0.5.1 → v0.5.2 refinements + bundle 008 promote (`_proposals/008_2026-06-03_hyperbrief-adoption/`): H2 status-based template selection + new compact BlockedStub templates / H3 self-contained `--help` clarity / H5 essence_one_line heading-strip / H6 plugin README catch-up sync / M4 new §8.5 sub-section codifying Hyperbrief's relation to Constellation §13.17 (main-chat structured-choice prohibition) and §13.18 (autonomous-execution absolute principle).** Bundle 008 absorption sweep. The downstream adopter's Hyperbrief-adoption dogfooding bundle (the H1 blocker landed as v2.5.32) ships the remaining 4 refinements + 1 cross-module clarification with no further blockers. **Bundle promoted** — `assets/reports/2026-06-03_hyperbrief-adoption/` (staging) → `_proposals/008_2026-06-03_hyperbrief-adoption/` (tracked) per staging note's "bundle 합류 또는 별도 bundle"; the bundle ships with `001_findings.md` (H1–H6 detailed + positives + priority recommendations) and a Korean `README.md`. **H2** (Med, code + templates) — `mini-engine.cjs` previously rendered every IR through `brief.{md,html}.template` regardless of the IR's `status` field, so a `BlockedStub` IR (`status: 'blocked_low_escalation'` — agent decided autonomously) rendered through the `FullBrief` template, producing empty fields for `Reversibility / Decider / Recommender / Deadline / Reading time` AND an irrelevant "⚠ Low-confidence brief" banner (the BlockedStub has neither those fields nor the `epistemic_distribution` the banner reads). Schema declares `oneOf [FullBrief, BlockedStub]` but the renderer ignored the variant. Two new templates `templates/brief-stub.md.template` + `templates/brief-stub.html.template` (compact post-notify card — escalation 4-score + sum + `autonomy_refusal_reason` + `autonomous_action_taken` + `post_notify_message`; one-screen surface; explanatory footer guiding how to force a FullBrief if needed). New `selectTemplate(ir, surface)` function picks the correct template based on `ir.status === 'blocked_low_escalation'`. Smoke test confirms BlockedStub renders the compact card (epistemic tag `[verified]` correctly transformed to `확인됨 —` at audience L2; determinism PASS on both surfaces — `md run1==run2 = f1e912d0aff8ea39`, `html run1==run2 = 202c9e5e5257270d`). **H3** (Low, CLI) — `bin/render.cjs --help` previously advertised `--self-contained` without indicating its v0.4.3-deferred status; the flag was a no-op that only logged a stderr warning ("inline asset bundling is deferred"). The `--help` string now reads `--self-contained (deferred to v0.4.3 — emits stderr warning, output still references CDN)` so adopters reading `--help` know it's not yet effective. Hard-fail considered but rejected — many adopters set the flag preemptively as a stylistic preference, and silent-deferred-warn preserves their workflow without forcing them to remove and re-add the flag at v0.4.3. **H5** (Low, renderer) — `section_6_decision_prompt.essence_one_line` carries the canonical epistemic-tag prefix (`[verified|inferred|assumed|unknown]`) in the IR (it's a `tagged_text` per `§5.1`), but the rendered MD H1 heading received that tag verbatim — e.g., `# ADR-hb-... — [verified] 결정 위임을 ...`. The tag is doughnut-chart metadata, not heading content. New `stripHeadingEpistemicTag(ir)` runs at the start of `renderMd` and `renderHtml` and strips the canonical bracket form (and the optional provenance bracket form) from `essence_one_line` only. The IR's field is mutated (per the §5.6.6 surface-vs-field separation), but `epistemic_distribution` and AF-18 estimate read from other fields, so the chart-tier signals are unaffected. **H6** (Low, doc) — `plugins/hyperbrief/README.md` was historically "Phase 1 prototype (v0.1.0)" — the v2.5.28 cut bumped `plugin.json` to v0.4.2 (and v2.5.30 to v0.5.0, v2.5.32 to v0.5.1) without touching the README. The README is now rewritten as `# Hyperbrief plugin — Phase 2 production (v0.5.2)` with a top-of-file callout noting the historic drift and the v0.5.2 catch-up; the "무엇을 주는가" section now describes the deterministic Node renderer + MCP server (both shipped at Phase 2) + the new BlockedStub templates; "Infrastructure requirements" reframed from "Phase 2 will add the renderer" to "renderers + mcp both shipped + single ajv ^8.17.0 dep" + active Constellation §13.16.9 / Superscalar §3.1 synergies. **M4** (Med, cross-module) — `Hyperbrief.md` gains new sub-section §8.5 "Constellation autonomous-execution layer — relation to §13.17 / §13.18" that codifies the boundaries between the three sections: §13.17 = first-move surface (no forced menus on contact); §13.18 = autonomous-execution absolute principle (gating conditions enumerated); Hyperbrief = post-§13.18-pass structured brief (output discipline once gating fires). The three cover disjoint surfaces — §13.18's four gating conditions map to Hyperbrief's MUST-trigger conditions, and §13.18 governs whether to ask while Hyperbrief governs how to ask once the answer is "yes, ask". Closes the bundle 007 M4 ask ("Constellation §13.17/§13.18 과의 중첩 범위를 어댑터가 직접 매핑해야 함") — adopters no longer need to derive the cross-section boundaries themselves. **Hyperbrief frontmatter** `version: v0.5.1 → v0.5.2` + status string rewritten to list the 5 refinements + bundle 008 absorption attribution. **Plugin manifest + sibling package.json** all bump `0.5.1 → 0.5.2` (plugin / renderers / mcp). **Scope discipline**: 2 new templates (`brief-stub.md.template` + `brief-stub.html.template`) + `mini-engine.cjs` (3 small functions: `stripHeadingEpistemicTag` + `selectTemplate` + each render entry-point's 2-line additions) + `bin/render.cjs` (1-line `--help` change) + `plugins/hyperbrief/README.md` (full rewrite to catch up Phase 2 surface) + `Hyperbrief.md` (§8.5 new sub-section + frontmatter) + version bumps (1 plugin manifest + 2 package.json + 1 frontmatter) + new `_proposals/008_2026-06-03_hyperbrief-adoption/{001_findings.md, README.md}`. - **v2.5.32** (2026-06-03) — **Hyperbrief v0.5.0 → v0.5.1 emergency-fix — clean-install ajv blocker (bundle 007 H1): `mini-engine.cjs` + `mcp/server.cjs` ajv import switched from default draft-07 entrypoint (`require("ajv")`) to draft-2020-12 dialect entrypoint (`require("ajv/dist/2020")`). Determinism PASS re-verified post-fix.** 2-line emergency-fix release. Bundle 007 (Hyperbrief adoption dogfooding from a downstream adopter) surfaced a blocker: `ajv` 8.x default export is the draft-07 dialect, but `hyperbrief.schema.json` declares `"$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema"` — so `ajv.compile(schema)` throws `no schema with key or ref draft/2020-12/schema` on every IR, breaking the validation-on default code path entirely. The adopter could render only with `--skip-validate`; shipped packages installed via `npm install` could not validate at all. The v0.4.0 determinism smoke test PASSED because it was run with `--skip-validate` against an already-vendored older ajv resolution; clean-install adopters did not have that escape. **The fix** is the 1-line import change per file (×2 files: renderers + mcp), with an inline comment explaining why the default draft-07 entrypoint is wrong for this schema's dialect. **Reproduction**: smoke test re-run with real `ajv ^8.17.0` installed in a clean node_modules confirms (a) compile no longer throws, (b) validation-on render proceeds normally, (c) IR-content schema enforcement now catches per-field violations as designed (the test ran against a sample IR with deliberate epistemic-tag gaps, ajv flagged each at correct path); determinism re-verified PASS (`md run1==run2` byte-identical, `html run1==run2` byte-identical — hashes match v0.5.0 post-button-label baseline). **Why a separate cut rather than folding into v2.5.33/.34**: H1 is a clean-install blocker for every adopter pulling EG @ v2.5.30; folding it into a larger Constellation/Hyperbrief refinement sweep would delay the fix availability. The bundle 007 + bundle 006 absorption sweeps follow as v2.5.33 + v2.5.34. **Hyperbrief frontmatter** `version: v0.5.0 → v0.5.1` + status string rewritten to flag the v0.4.0 smoke harness gap (smoke ran with `--skip-validate`, missed this) and the v0.5.1 emergency-fix cut ahead of bundle 007 absorption. **Plugin manifest + sibling package.json** all bump `0.5.0 → 0.5.1` (plugin / renderers / mcp). **Scope discipline**: 2-line code change (renderers/mini-engine.cjs + mcp/server.cjs, each 1 import line + a one-line inline comment) + version bumps (1 frontmatter + 3 package.jsons) + this CHANGELOG entry. (2) **`hyperbrief_validate`** — runs ajv against `schema/hyperbrief.schema.json`; lazy validator instantiation + graceful fallback when ajv not installed (returns `{ok: true, skipped: true, reason}` rather than failing hard); returns `{ok, skipped, ir_hash, errors[]}` with each error carrying `{path, message, keyword, params}`. Malformed rows skipped silently. **Constellation MCP server-side ack-tier extension** — `plugins/constellation/mcp/server.cjs` `handleMessage` ack-resolver branch for `Report` / `DONE` / `BLOCKED` / `NEEDS_HUMAN` extends to also match `DECISION_RESPONSE` / `DECISION_DEFER` / `DECISION_REJECT_FRAMING`; resolver logic distinguishes `tier='application'` (resolves on any of the seven outcomes) from `tier='decided'` (resolves only on the three DECISION_* outcomes). - **v2.5.24** (2026-06-03) — **Hyperbrief v0.1.1 → v0.4.0 — Phase 2 deterministic renderer shipped (`plugins/hyperbrief/renderers/`: `mini-engine.cjs` self-engineered placeholder substitution + tone-axis transform + canonical IR hash + ajv schema validation, `types.d.ts` interface contract, `bin/render.cjs` CLI entry point, `package.json` declaring single dep `ajv ^8.17.0`). This cut closes the renderer-absent interval that the v0.1.1 SSoT specified in `§10.3 Phase 1 transition rules` — the LLM no longer free-writes MD/HTML; it emits JSON IR only, and the deterministic Node renderer produces the MD/HTML. **4 renderer files** (`plugins/hyperbrief/renderers/`): (1) **`mini-engine.cjs` (~210 LoC)** — `canonicalIrHash` (stable JSON serialization with sorted keys at every depth → same logical IR → same hash) + `getValidator` / `validateIr` (ajv lazy load + graceful fallback when ajv not installed) + `substitute` (PLACEHOLDER_RE `\{\{([^}]+)\}\}` + auto-escape per surface) + 3 tone-axis transforms (`applyAudienceTransform` — L1-L2 epistemic bracket tags → Korean word forms `확인됨 / 추론 / 가정 / 미상`, L4-L5 → superscript shorthand `ᵛ ⁱ ᵃ ᵘ`; `applyAbbreviationTransform` — L3 bullet-first, L4+ telegraphic with `vs` `→` `∵` `∴` symbolic operators; `applyJargonTransform` — L1-L2 first-occurrence gloss via `JARGON_GLOSS` dict for RAPID / Cynefin / MCDA / Toulmin / blast radius / idempotent / Hyrum) + both `renderMd` / `renderHtml` surfaces + warnings accumulation + `resolveProfile` (override > IR > DEFAULT_PROFILE `{2,2,2}` with 1-5 clamp). (2) **`types.d.ts` (41 LoC)** — `AudienceProfile` `{audience, abbreviation, jargon: 1|2|3|4|5}` + `AudienceProfileFallback` + `HyperbriefIR` + `RenderResult` `{output, output_hash, ir_hash, audience_profile_applied, warnings[]}` + `RendererOptions` `{audience_profile_override?, self_contained_assets?, skip_validate?}` + `renderMd` / `renderHtml` / `canonicalIrHash` declared signatures + `McpRenderToolInput` for v0.4.1 MCP exposure. (3) **`bin/render.cjs` (~116 LoC)** — CLI entry point with `--format md|html` · `--ir <path>` (or stdin) · `--audience N` · `--abbreviation N` · `--jargon N` · `--self-contained` · `--skip-validate` · `--help`; exit codes 0 OK / 1 IR read failure / 2 schema validation failure / 3 unknown format; stderr emits `[warning] <msg>` for non-fatal renderer warnings. (4) **`package.json`** — name `@hyperbrief/renderers` · version `0.4.0` · private · main `./mini-engine.cjs` · types `./types.d.ts` · bin `hyperbrief-render` → `./bin/render.cjs` · single npm dep `ajv ^8.17.0` · engines `node >=18` · Apache-2.0. **Determinism smoke test (load-bearing v0.4.0 invariant per §7)**: rendering the same IR twice produces byte-identical output for both MD and HTML formats (verified — run1_hash == run2_hash for both surfaces using `bin/render.cjs --skip-validate` smoke harness). **§10.3 Phase 1 transition rules retained** (NOT deprecated, agent judgment per user delegation "(임시 patch 대체? 를 지금 할지는 네가 판단.)"): historical record value + external adopters won't migrate immediately so the fallback discipline retains value + preserving Phase 1 operational experience grounds future schema evolution + the drift-log's meaning naturally evolves into "Phase 1 template-substitute output vs Phase 2 renderer output backwards-compat regression verification". Body kept verbatim + one added **v0.4.0 status (2026-06-03 update)** paragraph stating the renderer ship fact and that new briefs after v0.4.0 SHOULD use mini-engine. **Hyperbrief.md frontmatter** v0.1.1 → v0.4.0 + status updated ("design draft v0.4.0 (Phase 2 — deterministic renderer shipped: plugins/hyperbrief/renderers/ mini-engine.cjs + types.d.ts + bin/render.cjs + package.json {dep: ajv ^8.17.0}; §10.3 Phase 1 transition rules retained with deprecation note)"). **dogfood ledger Entry 02 recorded** — decision_id `hb-20260603-r2nd02` · reversibility `one_way_with_migration_path` 🟡 · outcome accept (alternative B — self-built mini-engine + ajv + CLI; MCP tool exposure deferred to v0.4.1) · revisit 2026-09-01 · archive `_proposals/006_2026-06-03_hyperbrief/dogfood-entry-02.md`. **Entry 02 learnings (3 schema-gap candidates for future patches)**: (1) Declared vs effective `audience_profile` gap — the IR `audience_profile` is a *declaration* only, with no automated metric for whether the actual surface matches the declared level; root cause of this entry's R1 (declared L2 / effective L3-L4 with excessive English-jargon ratio) → R2 (L1/L1/L1 re-render); v0.5 candidate: add `surface_profile_estimate` (auto-computed jargon ratio / English-noun ratio / average sentence length) alongside `epistemic_distribution` + renderer warning when declared vs estimate gap > 1.0. - **v2.5.23** (2026-06-03) — **Hyperbrief v0.1.0 → v0.1.1 — new optional EG module + plugin scaffold (decision-delegation gating discipline). 6-axis deep research workflow synthesis (AI harness / humanities / psychology / management / philosophy / development; 6 parallel agents → barrier synth → design → proposal authoring → scaffold; ~861k subagent tokens), self-applied as dogfood Entry 01 with 5 patches landing in v0.1.1.** New top-level module — `Hyperbrief.md` SSoT (same EG-root tier as Constellation.md / Superscalar.md, governing the orthogonal "agent → user decision delegation" axis) + `plugins/hyperbrief/` (3 skills + IR schema + 2 templates + hooks placeholder) + `_proposals/006_2026-06-03_hyperbrief/` bundle (research bilingual + synthesis-and-design bilingual + dogfood-entry-01 archived). **Core thesis** (synthesis): Hyperbrief is a 5-stage pipeline disciplining "the very act of the AI asking the user for a decision" (trigger rubric → epistemic honesty → cognitive debiasing → reversibility-first governance → learning loop closure). **JSON IR + deterministic renderer separation** — the LLM emits only the IR, blocking MD/HTML drift (load-bearing). **§0 Decision Header** declares escalation 4-score + reversibility class + RAPID + Cynefin + decision_lineage + deadline + reading_minutes + stake + audience_profile (new in v0.1.1). **§7 Decision Tree** meta-branch (accept / reject_framing / defer / request_investigation) + 3 standardized root nodes (reversibility / blast_radius / time_pressure) + Cynefin-adaptive domain format. **§10 Normative rules**: 19 MUST + 7 SHOULD. **§6 Anti-patterns**: 23 AF (16 from v0.1 + 7 new in v0.1.1). **dogfood Entry 01 (self-application)** — applied the module to the read-through/approval decision for Hyperbrief.md v0.1 itself; the user decision cycle (sum=8/12 → FULL_HYPERBRIEF → alternative B accept) + 3 follow-up user prompts converted into 5 patches (P1+P2 user-explicit + P3+P4+P5 user-requested refinements) that landed in the v0.1.1 SSoT. **v0.1.1 patches**: (P1) **§11.3 cross-seed adoption** — `hb-uf-` / `hb-eg-` decision_id namespaces for EG-seed fork adapters like EstreUF + ledger separation + A2A intent sharing + schema version pinning discipline. (P2) **§10.3 Phase 1 transition rules** — operating rules for template-substitute mode during the renderer-absent v0.1.x ~ v0.4.0 window (IR-first invariant retained + template substitution enforced + drift-log telemetry + tone profile applied + self-throttle stays active). (P3) **§8 recommended_artifacts[] schema slot** (load-bearing) — closes the structural gap the user surfaced in the first briefing as "patch 본문이 어디 있어?"; mandates an IR slot for the artifact body attached to a recommendation `{artifact_type: patch|spec|code|design|config|other, target_file, target_anchor, body, rationale_one_line}` + MUST-18 + AF-20. (P4) **§5.6 audience_profile 3 axes × 5 levels + §5.6.7 tone-floor fallback affordance** — user fed back that the first briefing "전혀 눈에 안 들어와" → audience (L1 general / L2 general-dev mid default / L3 dev / L4 dev-expert mid / L5 expert-academic) · abbreviation (L1 full sentences / L2 light compression default / L3 bullet-heavy / L4 telegraphic / L5 spec-density) · jargon (L1 no jargon / L2 1-line gloss on first use default / L3 free / L4 framework cited / L5 terse citations) 3 orthogonal axes (collapsing into a single complexity score prohibited). **Tone-floor fallback** = always-visible HTML button ("뭔 소리야? 한국어로 번역해줘") + MD trigger phrases (`뭔 소리`, `안 읽혀`, `무슨 말`, `이해 안`, `더 쉽게`, `너무 어렵`, `다시 풀어`, `쉽게 다시`, `한국어로`, `한국말로`, `level 2 라고`, `L2 라고`, `이게 level`, `이게 L`) — re-render at `{1,1,1}` on auto-detection. (P5) **§9 archive_config** (optional, default ON) — archives a 5-element bundle (brief_original.md + decision.json + related_user_prompts.md + recommended_artifacts_applied.md + meta_learnings.md) on decision capture; archive_path defaults to `.agent/_decisions/<id>.archive/` or `_proposals/<bundle>/dogfood-entry-NN.md` (proposals-tracked). **Additional anti-patterns**: AF-17 (audience_profile missing/out-of-range) · AF-18 (surface vocab mismatch profile) · AF-19 (3 tone axes collapsed) · AF-20 (recommendation cites artifact but body missing) · AF-21 (HTML brief without tone-floor button) · AF-22 (MD brief: user confusion trigger but no regen) · AF-23 (decision archived but follow-up prompts not captured). **Additional normative rules**: MUST-16 (audience_profile required + 1-5 range) · MUST-17 (3 axes orthogonality) · MUST-18 (recommendation artifact disclosure) · MUST-19 (tone-floor fallback affordance) · SHOULD-5/6/7 (tone profile chip + abbreviation-aware prose style + jargon-aware glossing). **Workflow synthesis insight** (original draft's 8 sections → v0.1.1's 9 sections + IR + 5-stage pipeline): the 6-axis synthesis identified that the original draft's "force MD/HTML form output" pattern induces representation drift → evolved into schema-enforced JSON IR + deterministic renderer separation. Redefined the essential function from "help the user make decisions well" to "structurally block the agent from pulling the user into a sycophantic over-delegation loop". **dogfood ledger Entry 01 recorded** — decision_id `hb-20260603-a1b2c3` · reversibility `one_way_with_migration_path` 🟡 · outcome accept (alternative B + 5 patches) · revisit 2026-09-01 · archive `_proposals/006_2026-06-03_hyperbrief/dogfood-entry-01.md`. **Renderer (conversion tool) deferred to v2.5.24 (Phase 2 cut)** — this cut covers through the v0.1.1 SSoT + schema + skills + templates + dogfood archive; deterministic Node renderer (`renderers/`) + MCP tool exposure ship separately. **Scope discipline**: limited to the new module + plugin + proposal bundle. - **v2.5.22** (2026-06-02) — **constellation plugin v0.2.2 → v0.2.3: README "Infrastructure requirements" section added prominently for community-marketplace submission readiness; plugin manifest + marketplace description rewritten to disclose external-WS-server dependency upfront.** Plugin documentation patch — `plugins/constellation/README.md` gains a new prominent ⚠ section between the intro paragraph and "What this plugin gives you", spelling out the three runtime requirements (WS server at `CONSTELLATION_WS_URL`; state file at `CONSTELLATION_STATE_PATH`; role-keyed auth via `CONSTELLATION_TOKEN` / `_UPSTREAM_KEY` / `_COLLAB_KEY`), explaining what the plugin does WITHOUT a running server (loads clean, skills are docs-only, hook degrades gracefully, MCP tool calls fail with connection errors), and explaining why the architecture chooses external infra over a bundled default server (Constellation is a peer-coordination layer; the WS server holds shared state across agents, so bundling a single-process default server would defeat the multi-agent purpose). The README also adds a `What's in v0.2.3` and a backfilled `What's in v0.2.2` section (the v0.2.2 README sync from v2.5.20 was bundle-only and did not include a release-notes section in the README itself). Plugin manifest (`plugins/constellation/.claude-plugin/plugin.json`) and marketplace entry (`.claude-plugin/marketplace.json`) bump from v0.2.2 to v0.2.3; the marketplace description is rewritten to lead with "Live multi-agent orchestration *client* for Claude Code. Connects to a separately-running Constellation WebSocket server (user-provisioned; canonical reference impl at constellation/reference/runtime/server.cjs in this repo)" so the external-infra requirement is visible in the marketplace UI before install. **Trigger** — community-marketplace submission readiness research (this session's (c) workstream). Anthropic does not publish an explicit policy on plugins with external infrastructure dependencies, but the official `claude-plugins-official` marketplace already lists multiple precedents (Airtable, MongoDB, PostgreSQL, GitHub, Stripe — all of which connect to user-managed accounts / services / databases external to the plugin install), and the Claude Code MCP documentation explicitly endorses remote MCP servers (HTTP / SSE / WebSocket) as a standard supported transport. The conclusion is that infrastructure-dependent plugins are accepted; the submission-readiness work is therefore (a) explicit upfront disclosure in README + marketplace description and (b) clear graceful-degradation messaging — both of which v0.2.3 delivers. **Scope discipline**: plugin documentation + manifest version bumps only. Plugin source code (`mcp/server.cjs`, `hooks/pre-send-probe.cjs`, skills) unchanged. Constellation.md body unchanged. Reference-runtime unchanged. Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` — community-marketplace submission readiness cut.
- **v2.5.21** (2026-06-02) — **Constellation `§13.9.1` AgentHello opt-in broadcast presence + `§13.9.2` canonical-id alias discipline + `§13.13` layer-split normative clarification for gateway / adapter (Hermes 2nd handoff bundle review reflection).** Spec-body patch — `Constellation.md` gains two new sub-sections under §13.9 + one paragraph extending §13.13 "Layer split" to gateway / adapter implementations. Frontmatter `version: v2.3.18 → v2.3.19` + status string gains three new fragments. Reference-runtime unchanged. Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged. **Trigger** — 2026-06-01 Hermes 2nd handoff bundle (3 outer files + 9 inner ZIP files, sha256 anchor `2c370b…` byte-exact match, byte-verified in v2.5.18 S5 cycle) included three EG-side SSoT reflection asks from its MD section 5 review: explicit ack-semantic ownership rule extended to adapters / gateways (not just bridges), main-agent alias discipline for adopter identity layering, and AgentHello presence as opt-in broadcast rather than required handshake step. **§13.13 layer-split clarification** — the existing "bridge does NOT auto-emit `AckProcessed` / `Pong`" prohibition is extended explicitly to "every layer that sits between the agent's active runtime turn and the WS server — bridges, gateway adapters (Python `websockets`, Discord / Telegram / Slack platform adapters, IPC sidecars, any other proxy / connector / shim)." Discriminator is the owner of the agent-layer commitment signal, not the implementation language; same failure mode applies regardless of layer. **§13.9.1 AgentHello opt-in broadcast presence** — strict required handshake is `SERVER_HELLO` + `HELLO`; `AgentHello` is opt-in broadcast presence that (a) declares display metadata and (b) triggers receiver-bridge `OnboardAck` auto-emit. Adopters MAY skip when broadcast presence is undesirable (headless / stealth / telemetry-only / ephemeral debug); skipping yields a working connection without display metadata or auto-OnboardAck-driven worker standby. Discipline: when sent, MUST follow §2 step 3 wire shape; for `upstream` / `collab` MUST be broadcast (no specific `targetAgentId`); MUST NOT be used as a directed DM to `main-agent` (that misuse drives the alias-confusion failure mode below). Default for autonomous-peer / upstream-adapter implementations is `announce_agent_hello: false`. Constellation reference `local-bridge.cjs` sends by default because its canonical deployment is the interactive local-IDE worker pattern — that default is a property of the reference implementation, not of the protocol. **§13.9.2 Canonical-id + alias discipline** — canonical agentId (sent in `HELLO.agentId`) is the single source of truth for identity at the wire level; server has no built-in alias resolution. Adopters MAY operate aliases (e.g., treat `main-agent` placeholder as an alias for their actual canonical id) handled at the adapter layer. Adopter discipline: inbound target-alias SHOULD route to canonical; inbound source-alias + target-canonical MUST be treated as self-loop and dropped (recursive-wake prevention); outbound traffic MUST stamp canonical id (not alias) at `agentId` / `source`; dashboards SHOULD render `AgentList` rows by canonical id (alias is implementation detail). Named failure mode prevented: **alias-confusion** — an adapter treating `main-agent` as a separate peer, sending `AgentHello` as DM to it, receiving auto-`OnboardAck` for an identity that does not exist, with the live-board UI rendering the same agent twice (canonical + alias) and no error surface. **Scope discipline**: spec-body patch only (~3 paragraphs in §13.13 + two new sub-sections in §13.9 + frontmatter version bump + status string). Reference-runtime unchanged (existing `local-bridge.cjs` continues to behave as-is; the §13.9.1 default-send is preserved as the reference's deployment choice). Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` — Hermes-feedback-driven SSoT clarification is a minor cut.
- **v2.5.20** (2026-06-02) — **Constellation `§13.16.9` A2A-intent allowlist extension + doubly-wrapped envelope inner-name fallback in `pre-send-probe.cjs` (plus constellation plugin v0.2.1 → v0.2.2 bundle sync).** Reference-runtime patch — `constellation/reference/runtime/stop-hook/pre-send-probe.cjs` + bundled copy at `plugins/constellation/hooks/pre-send-probe.cjs`. **ALLOWLIST extension** — five new A2A-intent names added: `Request` / `Reply` (generic ask/respond envelopes used in cross-agent S4-style coordination), `Attachment` (standalone attachment metadata envelope per the Hermes 2026-06-01 11:09-11:11 UTC pattern), and `ArtifactManifest` / `ArtifactComplete` (chunked-transfer anchors per §13.11 rule 5; `ArtifactChunk` deliberately excluded as high-volume reassembly state rather than meaningful agent-layer signal). **Inner-name fallback** — the probe now also checks `value.name` for doubly-wrapped envelopes where the outer `name` field carries the literal string `"CUSTOM"` rather than the MessageName. This was observed in the 2026-06-02 Hermes meta-ack at inbox line 22856 and again at line 22858: Hermes-side envelope construction stamps `type: "CUSTOM"` at the outer name level and the actual MessageName (`Reply` or `Report`) at `value.name`. Without the fallback the cycle-end probe missed these envelopes entirely. The fallback is conservative: it only matches when the outer name is exactly `"CUSTOM"` (or absent) AND the inner name is in the allowlist — well-formed envelopes are unaffected. **Constellation plugin v0.2.2** absorbs the bundled probe-script update (no other plugin changes). **Scope discipline**: reference-runtime patch only (~10 lines added to `pre-send-probe.cjs` + bundled copy + plugin manifest version bumps in `plugins/constellation/.claude-plugin/plugin.json` and `.claude-plugin/marketplace.json`). Constellation.md body unchanged (§13.16.9 specifies the 4-group classification at a high level; the script implementation's specific allowlist is operational, extended in lockstep with discovered envelope patterns). Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` — user-directed allowlist extension is a minor cut.
- **v2.5.19** (2026-06-02) — **Constellation `§13.13.2` v0.5 reference impl bug fixes — server.cjs `_relayPendingClear` queue-key fix + local-bridge.cjs `delivered-persist` emit gated on `RELAY_REDELIVERY=on`.** Reference-runtime patch — `constellation/reference/runtime/server.cjs` + `constellation/reference/runtime/local-bridge.cjs`. Constellation.md body unchanged (v0.5 contract codified in v2.5.17 is correct; this version fixes implementation defects in the v2.5.15 reference). Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged. **Trigger** — 2026-06-02 dogfood on the hub: main found that its v2.5.15-derived `server.cjs._relayPendingClear` was looking up the wrong queue (key = `tgt` = `AckProcessed.targetAgentId` = original *sender* of the acked message, not the queue key which is the *recipient* = the AckProcessed *sender*). Pre-fix the lookup silently missed every commitment-tier clear, so even normal v0.5 first-receipt envelopes accumulated pending entries that aged into redelivery → false `RelayUnreachable{commitment-ack-absent}`. Main fixed the equivalent line on its own server and the dogfood subsequently passed (see v2.5.17 changelog). Main observed the EG reference `server.cjs` has the same line shape and recommended the same fix. Main also flagged a second issue: the EG bridge emitted `AckProcessed{tier:delivered-persist}` unconditionally, even with `RELAY_REDELIVERY=off`, producing board noise when the server's pending queue was dormant; main's own bridge gated the emit by `process.env.RELAY_REDELIVERY === 'on'`. Both fixes are bundled in v2.5.19. **server.cjs fix** (~line 442-445): the AckProcessed inbound branch's pending-clear call changes from `_relayPendingClear(tgt, msg.value.ackFor)` to `_relayPendingClear(conn.meta.agentId, msg.value.ackFor)` — `conn.meta.agentId` is the AckProcessed *sender* (= the original *recipient* of the acked message = the queue key under which the pending entry was registered). A multi-line code comment now records the bug and the fix rationale at the call site. **local-bridge.cjs fix** (~line 136, the v2.5.18 `delivered-persist` emit branch): the condition `appended && m.msgId && !_BRIDGE_ACK_KINDS.has(m.name)` gains a leading `process.env.RELAY_REDELIVERY === 'on'` gate. With redelivery off, no pending entry needs clearing and the emit is pure board noise; the gate prevents noise without changing v0.5 correctness when the redelivery scheduler is active. **§13.15 syntax gate**: `node --check` passes on both files. **Scope discipline**: reference-runtime patch only (~12 lines net change in server.cjs + ~3 lines net change in local-bridge.cjs, both inside existing branches). Constellation.md unchanged (v0.5 contract is correct; this is implementation hygiene). Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` — main-authorised reference-impl bug-fix cut.
- **v2.5.18** (2026-06-02) — **Constellation `§13.13.2` v0.5 reference implementation — bridge inbox-append commitment hook (EG-side complement to v2.5.17 spec).** Reference-runtime patch — `constellation/reference/runtime/local-bridge.cjs` `onInbound` gains a `delivered-persist` emit after successful inbox-append; §13.13.2 header comment updated to v0.4/v0.5 evolution. Constellation.md body unchanged (v0.5 spec already codified in v2.5.17). Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged (the `tier` field added per v2.5.17 spec is optional and back-compatible). **Trigger**: v2.5.17 spec patch ships the v0.5 contract; this version is the EG-side bridge reference implementation. Main's own bridge (`ws-local-bridge.cjs`) was updated independently and shipped at PID 437484 ahead of EG; this commit is the EG-repo complement so adopters cloning the canonical reference runtime get the v0.5 behaviour. **local-bridge.cjs change** (~20 lines inside `onInbound`, between the existing dedup branch at line 109 and the AgentHello auto-handler): on every CUSTOM inbound that passes dedup AND carries a `msgId` AND is NOT in `_BRIDGE_ACK_KINDS` (`Ack` / `AckProcessed` / `Ping` / `Pong` — never ack-the-ack), AND whose inbox.jsonl append succeeded, emit `CUSTOM/AckProcessed { ackFor: msgId, tier: "delivered-persist" }` targeted at the original sender (resolved as `m.agentId || m.value.agentId`, identical to the existing dedup-emit path). The emit composes with the v0.4 LRU dedup at line 109: duplicates emit `dedupHit:true` (v0.4 path, no `delivered-persist`); first-receipts emit `delivered-persist` (v0.5 path); the two never collide. **What this does NOT change**: the agent-layer application-tier ack discipline (`Report` / `DONE` / `BLOCKED` per §13.13) remains agent-emitted on its own dimension; the v0.5 `delivered-persist` ack lives on the *delivery* dimension and is bridge-emitted on its own authority. An agent that ALSO emits a v0.4-style commitment-tier `AckProcessed` is still spec-compliant — the server observes the pending entry already cleared by `delivered-persist` and treats the commitment ack as informational. **§13.15 syntax gate**: `node --check constellation/reference/runtime/local-bridge.cjs` passes. **Scope discipline**: reference-runtime patch only (~20 lines added to local-bridge.cjs + ~9-line comment update on the §13.13.2 dedup block). Constellation.md unchanged. Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` — main-authorised v0.5 reference impl is a minor cut.
- **v2.5.17** (2026-06-02) — **Constellation `§13.13.2` v0.4 → v0.5 spec patch — bridge inbox-append commitment + `delivered-persist` ack subtier (eliminates false-positive `RelayUnreachable{commitment-ack-absent}`).** Spec-body patch — `Constellation.md` §13.13.2 sub-section header bumped from `(v0.4 draft)` to `(v0.5)` + three new paragraphs (g) bridge inbox-append commitment + (h) tier-semantics vocabulary table + (i) migration path v0.4 → v0.5. Frontmatter `version: v2.3.17 → v2.3.18` + status line gains `at-least-once relay reliability v0.5 (§13.13.2 — bridge inbox-append commitment)`. Reference implementation ships separately as v2.5.18 EG-side complement. Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged (optional `tier` field added to `AckProcessed.value`, back-compatible). **Trigger** — 2026-06-02 dogfood: relay RRP §13.13.2 v0.4 hub adoption immediately after v2.5.15 ship surfaced a false-positive class — a normal `Ack` from EG → main was redelivered 3× → `RelayUnreachable{commitment-ack-absent}` despite the body having reached main's inbox file on the first attempt, because main's agent layer did not happen to emit a commitment-tier `AckProcessed` for it (agent idle / processing unrelated work). Main paused redelivery to OFF gate (`RELAY_REDELIVERY=off`) + proposed v0.5: bridge emits the commitment ack on its own authority immediately after inbox-append, since the bridge owns the persistence guarantee and the agent layer's commitment is properly an *outcome* signal not a *delivery* signal. EG agreed with all five arguments (false-positive removal · bridge always alive · v0.4 LRU dedup composes · agent layer keeps application-tier ack only · inbox-append IS the at-least-once anchor); main implemented main bridge v0.5 + restarted (PID 437484) + granted EG autonomous authority to ship spec patch + EG-side reference impl. **§13.13.2 (g) Bridge inbox-append commitment** — codifies the v0.5 contract: every successful inbound `CUSTOM` body that the recipient's bridge appends to its inbox file MUST be followed within milliseconds by `AckProcessed { ackFor: msgId, tier: "delivered-persist" }` emitted to the sender. Bridge does NOT wait for agent layer to read or process; the moment the body is durably persisted, the bridge has fulfilled its half of the at-least-once contract. Server treats `tier:"delivered-persist"` as the canonical pending-queue clear trigger, semantically equivalent to v0.4's commitment-tier ack but emitted by the transport layer that actually owns the persistence guarantee. **§13.13.2 (h) Tier semantics** — v0.5 distinguishes three named tiers with explicit emitter/trigger/pending-clear columns: `delivered` (server-emitted, wire received, no pending clear) · `delivered-persist` (bridge-emitted, inbox-append complete, canonical pending clear) · `commitment` (agent-emitted, body surfaced into working context, redundant after `delivered-persist`). Application-tier outcomes (`Report` / `DONE` / `BLOCKED` per §13.13) live on a separate outcome dimension; v0.4 `AckProcessed` without `tier` field is interpreted as `commitment` for back-compat (a v0.4 receiver paired with v0.5 server continues to operate at v0.4 semantics, including the false-positive class — the escape requires the v0.5 *bridge*). **§13.13.2 (i) Migration path** — per-component update: server gains "delivered-persist clears pending entry" rule (additive over v0.4 commitment-tier clear) + optional per-target `RELAY_REDELIVERY=off` gate (operators disable redelivery while v0.5 bridges roll out); bridge adds inbox-append hook with immediate `delivered-persist` emit (composes with v0.4 §13.13.2(c) LRU dedup — duplicates still emit `AckProcessed{ackFor, dedupHit:true}` without inbox-append, so no `delivered-persist` for duplicates); agent unchanged (mechanism is bridge-layer, invisible to agent code). **Empirical validation** — 2026-06-02 dogfood with main-EG bidirectional: main's bridge added the hook + restart (PID 437484) + the next EG → main envelope cleared pending in <1s without redelivery or `RelayUnreachable`. EG-side reference impl (the v2.5.18 ship) is the EG bridge complement. **Scope discipline**: spec-body patch only (~3 paragraphs added to §13.13.2 sub-section + header version bump + frontmatter). Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged (optional `tier` field added to `AckProcessed.value` is back-compatible per §13.13 — receivers and intermediate proxies that ignore the field continue to function at v0.4 semantics). Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` — main-authorised v0.5 spec patch is a minor cut.
- **v2.5.16** (2026-06-02) — **`docs/promo/` — EstreGenesis + Superscalar + Constellation public promo site (GitHub Pages publishable; bilingual EN/KO + theme switcher).** (See KO block for details — this is the same v2.5.16 entry already codified below; full English entry was earlier folded under the v2.5.16 polish cut.)
- **v2.5.15** (2026-06-02) — **Constellation `§13.13.2` v0.4 reference implementation — server pending queue + redelivery scheduler + RelayUnreachable emit + bridge LRU dedup with `dedupHit:true` AckProcessed.** Reference-runtime patch — `constellation/reference/runtime/server.cjs` + `constellation/reference/runtime/local-bridge.cjs`. Constellation.md body unchanged (the §13.13.2 contract codified in v2.5.11 is the spec; this version is its reference implementation per the §13.13.2 Phase 2 deferred-list). Seed lib unchanged. Triggered by user instruction ("바로 진행하지?"). **server.cjs additions** (`constellation/reference/runtime/server.cjs` ~lines 155-200 + relay branch): **(a) Pending queue** — `_relayPending` Map keyed by `targetAgentId`, FIFO per-target with cap `RELAY_PENDING_MAX=256` (env-overridable). Each entry `{ msgId, payload, firstAt, attempts, hasEmbeddedAttachment }`. Entries register on the relay branch whenever `wsIsAckable(msg)` returns true AND the target is connected — same gate as the transport-tier `Ack delivered` emit; the v0.3 baseline already filtered ack/ping/telemetry out of the pending track. **(b) Commitment-tier clear on AckProcessed** — when a `CUSTOM/AckProcessed` envelope is relayed with `value.ackFor` matching a pending entry's msgId AND a `targetAgentId` matching the original target, `_relayPendingClear(tgt, ackFor)` removes the entry. This is the key inversion vs v0.3: pending is cleared by commitment-tier ack (agent layer), NOT by transport-tier `Ack delivered` (server layer). **(c) Redelivery scheduler** — `setInterval(_relayScheduleTick, 10*1000)` scans pending entries every 10s; an entry past `RELAY_THRESHOLD_MS` (default 30s dogfood / 5min prod — env-overridable) AND recipient AgentList-present AND attempts < max → redeliver via `d.send(payload)` + increment attempts + reset firstAt. Recipient-absent → defer redelivery until reconnect. Max-attempts hit → emit `RelayUnreachable { msgId, targetAgentId, attemptCount, lastError }` to the **sender** (not broadcast — only the sender needs to know its message did not stick) + clear pending entry. The sender then escalates to human review per §13.13 application-tier ladder. **(d) §13.11 rule 5 attachment-aware throttle** — entries carrying `value.attachments[]` with any `source: "embedded"` (or any `dataUrl` field) attachment use `Math.ceil(max_attempts / 2)` as the effective cap (default 3 → 2 for embedded). Duplicate large payload redelivery is bandwidth-expensive + the receiver's msgId dedup catches it on first redelivery anyway; the throttle is the cost-asymmetry response. **(e) Scheduler unref'd** (`.unref()`) — does not keep the Node event loop alive past server shutdown. **local-bridge.cjs additions** (`constellation/reference/runtime/local-bridge.cjs` ~lines 75-104): **(f) LRU dedup with TTL** — `_seenMsgIds` upgraded from unbounded `Set` to `Map(msgId → seen-ts)` with `_SEEN_LRU_MAX=1024` entries + `_SEEN_TTL_MS=1h` per §13.13.2 v0.4 provisional defaults. `_dedupCheck(msgId)` performs TTL evict from oldest (Map insertion-order iteration is JS spec) + LRU evict on cap + insert/refresh. Returns true on duplicate. **(g) `dedupHit: true` AckProcessed emit** — when `_dedupCheck` returns true, the bridge emits `CUSTOM/AckProcessed { ackFor: <msgId>, dedupHit: true }` targeted at the original sender agent (`m.agentId || m.value.agentId`) + discards the body (no inbox.jsonl append, no agent layer surface). The sender's server-side `_relayPending` entry then clears via path (b) above. Without `dedupHit` emit, redelivery would loop indefinitely until max-attempts (RelayUnreachable false-alarm); with `dedupHit` emit, redelivery is server-side mechanic invisible to the agent layer (correct §13.13.2 semantic). **Env-overridable knobs**: `RELAY_PENDING_MAX` (default 256) · `RELAY_THRESHOLD_MS` (default 30000 = 30s; prod adopters set to 300000 = 5min) · `RELAY_MAX_ATTEMPTS` (default 3). Scheduler scan interval is hardcoded at 10s (sub-threshold; tunable in code). **What v2.5.15 does NOT add** (still §13.13.2 Phase 3 candidates): durable pending queue (in-memory only; server restart loses pending state — acceptable for dogfood, prod adopters add persistence) · cross-server pending state (single-server scope) · telemetry sink for redelivery/dedup-hit/RelayUnreachable rate calibration (logged via `console.warn` only) · per-target backpressure (a slow recipient just accumulates pending up to cap then FIFO-evicts oldest). **Composition tested**: PR #4/PR #5 trace would now also clear server pending on the manual fast-path PRMergeAck (which is application-tier, not commitment) — Phase 3 may add explicit application-tier pending clear OR rely on max-attempts timeout. For now, application-tier outcomes do NOT auto-clear pending (only commitment-tier does); long-running tasks should emit AckProcessed at acceptance time. **Scope discipline**: reference-runtime patch only (~70 lines added to server.cjs + ~25 lines added to local-bridge.cjs). Constellation.md body unchanged (§13.13.2 spec already codified at v2.5.11). Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged (server-side state keyed by existing `msgId` field per v0.4 contract). Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` — user-directed Phase 2 reference impl is a minor cut.
- **v2.5.14** (2026-06-02) — **A2A PR System RRP v0.3 → v0.4 DRAFT: `§10B Manual fast-path` codified (trusted-mirror short-circuit, PR #4 + PR #5 dogfood validation, dry-run draftRef consistency gate).** RRP-only patch — `constellation/reference/docs/2026-06-01-a2a-pr-system-rrp.md` body augmentation (new §10B sub-section between §10A and §11; v0.3 → v0.4 banner; status preamble updated). Constellation.md body unchanged. Seed lib unchanged. Protocol wire unchanged. **Trigger**: 2026-06-01 dogfood — PR #4 (`a3344d7`, §13.11 rule 5 + §13.13.2 RRP mirror, 40 ins) + PR #5 (`1e2c3f9`, §13.16.12 Pattern 7 mirror, 19 ins) both completed via a **single-envelope manual short-circuit** (PRRequest dry-run → PRMergeAck) rather than the §9/§10A canonical six-envelope chain (PRRequest + PRDraftReady×2 + PRRequest re-emit + PRReviewAck + PRMergeRequest + PRMergeAck). Main acknowledged the pattern + user authorised codification ("user decision to register d-pr-manual-fastpath + EG autonomous RRP permitted + redaction grep + dry-run draftRef consistency gate as mandatory codification conditions"). **§10B contract** (six sub-sections): **§10B.1 e2e diagram** of the short-circuit (PRRequest{dryRun:true} → bridge handlePrRequestL1 dry-run → PRDraftReady{dryRun:true, draftRef:'dryrun-<msgId>', checksPending:[]} → main manual `git append + add <targetPath> + commit + push origin main` → PRMergeAck{merged:true, dryRun:false, commit:<sha>, pushSuccess:true, draftRef:<dryrun consistent>, forMsgId:<msgId>}); collapses 8 envelopes (chain) to 2 envelopes (fast-path); operator's manual git step replaces the chain's PRReviewAck+PRMergeRequest+cherry-pick+push steps. **§10B.2 redundancy cost analysis** — table mapping each chain step's information contribution; PRReviewAck adds no new information for trusted-mirror (single-file append, redaction grep already in dry-run); the chain's redundancy is intentional for standard PRs (cross-cutting impact catch) but pure cost for trusted-mirror. Fast-path saves 6 envelopes + PR_LIVE state toggle. **§10B.3 use-criteria** (ALL required): category=trusted-mirror · kind=inline-section-mirror · mergeStrategy=append-section · single target file · dry-run draftRef present + consistent in PRMergeAck · redaction grep clean at dry-run · per-PR operator manual review. **§10B.4 do-NOT-use** for: standard/branch-ref/inline-files-diff PRs · multi-file · non-append-section mergeStrategy · shared mutable state (state.json/config/schema) · first-time adopter (loses dogfood signal). **§10B.5 dry-run draftRef consistency gate** (load-bearing invariant) — PRMergeAck.draftRef MUST match PRDraftReady.draftRef from the dry-run; without this, fast-path PRMergeAck is indistinguishable from an unauthenticated merge claim (anyone could synthesize merge confirmation). Bridge emits `dryrun-<msgId>` deterministically; main MUST carry verbatim. PR #4 trace: msgId `m-<id>` → draftRef `dryrun-constellatio-m-<id>` (dry-run) → same draftRef in PRMergeAck (manual merge). Verifiable from inbox.log alone. **§10B.6 composition** with §6 approval discipline (trusted-mirror per-PR opt-in still in force) + §13.14 redaction discipline (dry-run grep load-bearing) + §13.13.2 dedup (msgId-keyed; fast-path inherits dedup property) + §13.16.10 pre-send probe (operator's manual append step is preceded by their own probe) + §13.16.12 board render (PRMergeAck renders as A2A card; manual git ops are out-of-band side channel, acceptable). **§10B.7 dogfood evidence** — PR #4 + PR #5 two-case anchor table (both trusted-mirror, single-file append-section, dry-run clean, manual append+push, PRMergeAck draftRef consistent, zero regressions vs chain). **§10B.8 what fast-path does NOT codify** — single-axis short-circuit only; does not change wire vocabulary, approval discipline category enum, redaction discipline, dedup mechanic, or operator's manual review responsibility. Fast-path is *easier* not *less rigorous*. **Status preamble** (top of RRP): v0.3 → v0.4 + new banner line crediting §10B addition + PR #4/PR #5 dogfood + load-bearing dry-run draftRef invariant. **Version**: v0.4 DRAFT (2026-06-02). **Scope discipline**: RRP-only patch (~120 lines added). Constellation.md body unchanged. Seed lib unchanged. Protocol wire unchanged. Manual fast-path is a *delivery-side discipline*, not a wire-format change. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` — user-authorised RRP body augmentation cut.
- **v2.5.13** (2026-06-02) — **Constellation `§13.16.12 Pattern 7` — board render TEXT_MESSAGE fallback to A2A card (defense layer for non-conformant adopters).** Constellation patch — body-only augmentation (new pattern added to existing §13.16.12 sub-section under §13.16), no wire-format change, no seed cascade. Frontmatter `version: v2.3.16 → v2.3.17` + status string gains `board render TEXT_MESSAGE fallback (§13.16.12 Pattern 7)`. **Trigger**: 2026-06-01 dogfood — Hermes Dev Agent's ws_agent_client.py was diagnosed (main-side, sub-user-instruction inspection of `ws-history/hermes-dev-agent.jsonl`, ~200 lines) to emit ALL outbound A2A as `TEXT_MESSAGE` envelopes carrying serialized JSON in `.text` rather than structured `CUSTOM` envelopes with `value` + `attachments[]`. The Hermes side's R2 pending finding (ws_agent_client.py validation) confirmed at the byte level. Main shipped a render-tier defense layer at commit `5983f57` (app.js `wsExtractA2aReport` helper + TEXT_MESSAGE branch that promotes serialized JSON code blocks into `a2acard` rendering, Playwright-verified). User authorised the formalisation as a §13.16.12 Pattern 7 candidate; this version codifies it at the protocol tier so other Constellation adopters running similar implementations get the same defense layer. **Pattern 7 contract**: receiver-side dashboard MAY detect TEXT_MESSAGE envelopes whose `text` carries a serialized A2A Report (typically a `[A2A Report]` lead line followed by a fenced JSON code block with `{ type: "Report", ... }`) and **promote** the message into an A2A card render — extracting the JSON payload, parsing it, and rendering as if it had arrived as a native CUSTOM envelope. Implementation discipline: (1) detection runs as a `TEXT_MESSAGE` branch, after the normal text render is computed but before DOM commit; if extraction succeeds, surface swaps to A2A card; if extraction fails, message renders as normal TEXT_MESSAGE (graceful degradation, never errors loudly). (2) Promoted card MUST carry a `fallback` visual badge (small label or tooltip "promoted from TEXT_MESSAGE") so the operator can distinguish a canonical CUSTOM-rendered card from a Pattern-7-promoted card — preserves audit-trail integrity and surfaces which adopters remain non-conformant. (3) Promotion MUST NOT alter the outbound ack path (transport-tier Ack continues against the original TEXT_MESSAGE frame; commitment-tier AckProcessed follows §13.13 normally; promotion is render-layer only). (4) Promotion MUST extract `attachments[]` from the JSON when present + render chips per §13.11 rule 5 + Pattern 3 graceful-localPath discipline (Pattern 7 supplies the parsed array; Pattern 3 supplies the per-chip render discipline). **Composition**: §13.11.3 rule 1 (server stamps `type: "CUSTOM"` when absent) handles the *type-omitted* case; Pattern 7 handles the stronger *wrong-envelope-shape* case (sender wrapped the whole envelope into TEXT_MESSAGE). Pattern 6 (source-set-agnostic detection + text relay fallback) handles the *router*-side defect; Pattern 7 handles the *render*-side complement (TEXT_MESSAGE correctly routed but wrongly shaped). With the §13.16.10 pre-send probe: Pattern 7 promotion does NOT alter cursor advancement; Pattern-7-promoted cards count as meaningful inbound and the watcher / pre-send probe's A2A-intent allowlist SHOULD treat TEXT_MESSAGE-Pattern-7-detected as meaningful for adopters running the fallback. **Lifecycle expectation**: Pattern 7 is a **transitional defense layer**. Adopters view Pattern 7 hits as a backlog signal (each promoted card = an instance of a non-conformant producer needing fix). Discipline target: *zero Pattern 7 hits* over a steady operating window. When all adopters emit structured envelopes per §13.11, Pattern 7 becomes dormant but is NOT removed — it protects against regression. **Reference implementation**: upstream commit `5983f57` (app.js `wsExtractA2aReport` helper + TEXT_MESSAGE branch). The dashboard-render-patterns.md reference doc may grow a §9 "TEXT_MESSAGE-to-A2A-card fallback" section in a future revision to mirror this protocol-tier addition. **Scope discipline**: Constellation.md body augmentation only (one new pattern in existing §13.16.12 sub-section). Wire format unchanged (Pattern 7 is render-tier behavior — wire still emits TEXT_MESSAGE from the non-conformant producer; the receiver-side promotion is a render-layer recovery). Seed lib unchanged. `dashboard-render-patterns.md` reference doc unchanged in v2.5.13. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` — user-authorised defense-layer protocol body augmentation cut.

- **v2.5.11** (2026-06-02) — **Constellation `§13.13.2` at-least-once relay reliability RRP draft (server pending queue + redelivery + idempotent receiver dedup; v0.4 contract).** Constellation patch — body-only augmentation (new sub-section under §13.13), no wire-format shape change (server-side state keyed by existing `msgId` field; no envelope additions), no seed cascade. Frontmatter `version: v2.3.15 → v2.3.16` + status string gains `at-least-once relay reliability v0.4 draft (§13.13.2)`. **Trigger**: 2026-06-01 dogfood surfaced **3 relay-drop incidents within one cycle** (a24c5897 Hermes morning drop · Hermes 2nd handoff localPath drop · Hermes transport-mode negotiation drop), reaching the escalation threshold codified in `memory/feedback_a2a_relay_reliability.md` (1 cycle / 3 drops = RRP). Main acknowledged the threshold + user authorised the RRP (line 22765, 2026-06-01 15:20 UTC — "EG 자율 진행 OK + 시점 조율"). **The v0.4 contract** (additive, layered on top of v0.3 — wire envelope unchanged): **(a) Server-side pending queue** — server retains pending `{ msgId, targetAgentId, payload-hash, first-attempt-ts, attempt-count }` entry per targeted CUSTOM with msgId, FIFO per-target, default cap 256 entries / 30 min. Cleared on commitment-tier `AckProcessed` (NOT transport-tier `Ack delivered` — key inversion vs v0.3). **(b) Redelivery policy** — re-emit when first-attempt-ts exceeds threshold (default 5 min production / 30s dogfood — adopters tune). Bounded by attempt-count (max 3) AND recipient connection state (skip if not AgentList-present; defer until reconnect). After max attempts → `RelayUnreachable { msgId, targetAgentId, attemptCount, lastError }` emitted to the SENDER (not broadcast) + pending entry cleared. Sender escalates to human review via board `decisions` panel per §13.13 application-tier ladder. **(c) Idempotent receiver dedup** — bridge maintains seen-msgId LRU (default 1024 / 1 hour); duplicate msgId → emit `AckProcessed { ackFor, dedupHit: true }` immediately + discard duplicate body. Without dedup, redelivery would surface N copies; with it, redelivery is server-side mechanic invisible to the agent layer (except via the `dedupHit: true` flag for outcome tracking). **(d) Composition with v0.3 ack tiers** — three tiers preserved verbatim (transport · commitment · application); v0.4 changes WHEN server clears pending (commitment, not transport) + adds redelivery-on-absence-of-commitment that v0.3 lacks. Back-compatible: an adopter that has not migrated continues at-most-once; the wire requires no new fields (msgId already exists per v0.3 §13.13). **(e) Composition with §13.11 rule 5 attachment transport-mode** — embedded attachments raise redelivery cost; redelivery SHOULD apply attachment-aware throttle (half the standard max attempts for envelopes with `source: "embedded"` entries, since duplicate large payloads are bandwidth-expensive). Chunked transfer (`ArtifactManifest`/`ArtifactChunk`/`ArtifactComplete`) is independently idempotent at chunk level + does NOT participate in msgId pending queue at chunk granularity. **(f) Composition with broker-forward workaround** — the workaround codified in `memory/feedback_a2a_relay_reliability.md` (extract from main `ws-history/<sender-agentId>.jsonl` and forward to recipient) remains a valid manual escalation path even after v0.4 ships, for cases where pending queue exceeds cap or recipient stays disconnected past `RelayUnreachable`. Broker-forward emit carries original msgId, so recipient seen-msgId set deduplicates against the original delivery attempt — workaround does NOT bypass v0.4 dedup. **Phase 1 ship (this version)**: contract codified. **Phase 2 (v2.5.12+)**: reference implementation (server.cjs pending queue + redelivery scheduler + bridge dedup LRU) — sequenced after Hermes dataUrl reemit catch + Mode B baseline absorption per user-confirmed time scheduling. Provisional defaults (queue cap 256 · redelivery threshold 5min/30s · max attempts 3 · dedup-LRU 1024/1h) expect tuning after 1-2 weeks of v0.4 telemetry. **Scope discipline**: Constellation.md body augmentation only (one new sub-section under §13.13). Wire shape unchanged. Seed lib unchanged. Hub mirror via A2A PR #4 (per main's "PRRequest 시 허브 WS-PROTOCOL.md mirror" cadence) is a separate follow-up. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` — meaningful protocol body augmentation + user-authorised RRP cut.
- **v2.5.10** (2026-06-02) — **Constellation `§13.11 rule 5` attachment transport-mode discipline (`source` enum `local_path | embedded | url | chunked` + standard attachment-object fields + ack-tier semantics + Hermes-EG convergent ship).** Constellation patch — body-only augmentation, no wire-format shape change (attachment-object fields are additive), no seed cascade. Frontmatter `version: v2.3.14 → v2.3.15` + status string gains `attachment transport-mode v0.4 (§13.11 rule 5)`. New §13.11 rule 5 closes the cross-environment byte-transport gap surfaced by the Hermes 2nd handoff bundle (inbox lines 22702-22709, 2026-06-01 11:09-11:11 UTC) where `source: "local_path"` attachments did NOT transport bytes across the A2A gateway boundary (provenance metadata only — receivers cannot fetch the sender's local filesystem), producing a ~10-hour awareness delay + bodyPreview-only consolidation in v2.5.6. **Rule 5 specifies the `source` enum** (`local_path` = sender-filesystem provenance only · `embedded` = dataUrl base64-encoded bytes ≤24 MB practical inline payload, canonical default for cross-environment handoffs · `url` = external-hosted with signed/token-gated fetch for >24 MB or TTL-controlled artifacts · `chunked` = multi-message ArtifactManifest + ArtifactChunk + ArtifactComplete sequence for very large or retry-required transfers) + **standard attachment-object fields** (`name` · `mime` · `size` · `sha256` · `source` · `path` for sender-local provenance · `dataUrl`/`url`/`chunks[]` per source-type) + **hybrid embedded form** (canonical default: BOTH `path` (sender-local provenance/debug) AND `dataUrl` (authoritative transported bytes), receiver treats `dataUrl` as bytes source and `path` as metadata-only). Server MAX_BODY = 32 MB; base64 overhead ~33% means practical inline payload ≤24 MB. **Convergent ship coordination**: Hermes Dev Agent + EG converged on rule 5 independently during the 2026-06-01 dogfood cycle. EG outbox 295 (14:35 UTC) proposed four transport-mode options with `(d) hybrid` as the recommendation; Hermes line 199 (~15:00 UTC, forwarded by main-broker since the at-most-once relay dropped the substantive Report — recurrence of the relay-drop class observed earlier in the day, surfaced as a separate §13.x agenda item for at-least-once relay semantics) accepted `(d) hybrid localPath + dataUrl, source=embedded` as default for future handoffs and explicitly agreed to the §13.11 rule 5 codification ship at v2.5.10. **Ack-tier semantics for embedded attachments**: §13.13 transport-tier `Ack` = "envelope delivered to recipient's WS connection" (does NOT separately confirm decode or sha256-verify); commitment-tier `AckProcessed` SHOULD mean "received + decoded + sha256-verified + persisted" per receiver policy; application-tier (`Report` / `DONE`) carries the outcome of using the attachment (archive update, byte-verification pass/fail, regeneration request). Composes with §13.13 3-tier mapping without introducing a new tier. **Cross-link to §13.16.12 Pattern 3**: dashboard render-tier already specifies graceful localPath display (chip with "local file, not transported" indicator vs error/broken-link); rule 5 is the protocol-tier counterpart that Pattern 3's visualisation reflects. The two compose: §13.11 rule 5 = wire contract, §13.16.12 Pattern 3 = render contract. **Hermes reemit in-progress**: Hermes is verifying `/tmp/hermes` artifact presence and will either reemit the 2nd handoff bundle in the embedded form (md 9384B + diff patch 1811B + tar.gz 262KB as three `source: "embedded"` attachments with dataUrl + sha256) or surface artifact-missing fallback to operator/regeneration. EG-side will byte-decode + sha256-verify against HANDOFF-MANIFEST.json on receipt and update `constellation/reference/docs/2026-06-01_hermes/_2nd-handoff/` archive with verified bytes. **Composition with §8 MCP integration**: the MCP server skeleton (`plugins/constellation/mcp/server.cjs`, v2.5.9 Phase 1) handles the read interface today; chunked attachment transport via MCP is on §8.6 Phase 2 deferred-list. **Scope discipline**: Constellation.md body augmentation (one new rule in existing §13.11.3 sub-section). Wire shape unchanged (attachment-object fields are additive; `source` enum extends — `local_path` was already the de facto value). Seed lib unchanged. `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` alignment — convergent-evolution protocol body augmentation cut.
